Zhao Pi-lian Discusses: Communist Bandits in Shanxi Have Been Eliminated; Second Plenary Session May Not Be Able to Attend; Earnest Advice Has Been Given to the Two Guangdongs 17

(Nanjing) Zhao Pi-lian told reporters on the 30th that the Communist bandits in Shanxi have been eliminated, and local security has returned to its original state. Director Yan is now working hard to handle all the aftermath. Due to busy military and political affairs, he may not be able to come to Nanjing to attend the Second Plenary Session. Yan's attitude towards the current situation is that the national crisis in China is serious, and the whole country should take unified steps, and must not be divided or alienated, so as to reduce the national strength and create opportunities for others. As for the dispatch of troops by the two Guangdongs this time, he telegraphed to the authorities of the two Guangdongs, earnestly advising them to put the nation and the people first. There have long been rumors of unusual movements in Suiyuan and Mongolia. As for the truth, because there will be an official report at the meeting, the successor of the Chairman of the Chahar-Suiyuan Mongol Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee and League Chief of the Xilingol League, So Wang, who has passed away, is currently being considered for appointment by the central government. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 30th)

Wang Yong-bin Discusses Recent Work of the Ministry of Justice 18

(Nanjing) Minister of Justice Wang Yongbin discussed that the central work of the ministry in the past year has been to implement the new trial system nationwide, reform the principles of justice and the judicial system, reduce overcrowding in prisons, reduce detention in detention centers, and clear accumulated cases in various courts, with new cases being concluded as soon as they arrive. Regarding the first point, in addition to supervising and ordering the provinces implementing the new system to strengthen their organizations, we have repeatedly ordered the eight provinces that have been delayed to make thorough preparations, lest the preparations are not complete. Fortunately, Sichuan has added three higher branch courts and reorganized two, and added more than ten district courts. Guizhou has added two higher branch courts and three district courts. Yunnan has added one higher branch court and three district courts. Suiyuan has added one higher branch court and one district court. Qinghai has too few counties under its jurisdiction and does not need to add higher branch courts, but it has added one district court in Ledu. These five poor and remote provinces have all worked hard to prepare and implement the new system as scheduled. In addition, there are higher and district courts in the provincial capital of Xinjiang. Xinjiang has only one district court for thousands of miles, and it has been ordered to add higher branch courts to facilitate appeals by the people. Due to the lack of funds and personnel, it has not been possible to rush the preparations. As for Guangdong and Guangxi, they had already made full preparations, but the Southwest Government suddenly ordered them to postpone the implementation, probably because Article 21 of the Court Organization Law stipulates that the Supreme Court shall be located in the seat of the National Government. Once the new system is implemented, the so-called Supreme Branch Court will not be able to exist. Why preserve this unfounded branch court and make the national laws inconsistent? This is incomprehensible. Therefore, only five of the eight provinces have actually implemented the new system, which is very regrettable. The fact that the county magistrate also handles judicial affairs has not been improved for more than ten years, resulting in the fact that the facts of the cases in the first instance are not understood, and all hope to have the verdicts reversed in the second and third instances. Therefore, there are many appeals and heavy burdens. The Ministry of Justice believes that unless we engage in the reorganization of the first instance, our country's judiciary will never be clear, and decided to first establish the Regulations for the Organization of County Judicial Offices. On April 24, we ordered all provinces to prepare to reorganize the county judicial offices in three phases starting from July 1 this year, with each phase not exceeding six months. It is estimated that by the end of next year, the malpractice of the county magistrate concurrently handling judicial affairs in these more than 1,400 counties can be eliminated. In the past two months, more than ten provinces have formulated plans and complied with the reorganization in phases. The provinces of Shandong, Hubei, and Gansu have decided to correct all the county judicial offices in the province starting from July 1. The local administrative authorities and judicial officials are particularly courageous in reforming, but it is also sufficient to show that the concurrent system has been criticized by the world, and they only fear that it will not be eliminated quickly. The overcrowding in prisons and detention centers everywhere is unbearable, and dredging is an urgent problem. The purpose of execution in prison is reformation. If there is evidence of repentance, why wait for the completion of the sentence? Although the criminal law stipulates conditions for parole, it is still too strict. Therefore, we proposed special measures to dredge prisons, which were effective for six months, from July 25 last year to January 15 this year, and about 15,000 people were released. As for the dredging of detention centers, there are many methods stipulated in the law, but the judges are not responsible, and they arbitrarily detain people. In addition, the lawsuits are crowded and delayed, and the pain is even worse. The Ministry of Justice repeatedly warned them to carefully detain people, and those who have been detained should be released quickly if they are eligible for bail. In the past year, due to the large number of courts and the increase in criminal cases, the number of people detained has decreased significantly compared to the past. The large number of accumulated cases and the suffering of lawsuits have been called for by the whole country. Since November last year, we have set a deadline of six months to clear all accumulated cases nationwide, and use the results of clearing accumulated cases as the standard for annual performance appraisal. At the same time, we will compare and list the total number of cases received and concluded by each court each month and publish them in the Judicial Monthly. As of the end of April, the number of pending cases in courts at all levels was 22,855 civil cases and 11,223 criminal cases. If the average is calculated for 379 courts, then each court has no more than 60 civil cases and no more than 30 criminal cases. The prosecutor's office has only a few cases per court. These pending cases are either complicated and cannot be concluded quickly, or there are unexpected obstacles and are suspended according to law. Most of the accumulated cases have been cleared, and new cases have been concluded quickly, and there are no cases that have been accumulated for more than a year or several years. (Special dispatch on the 30th)

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan held its 18th regular meeting on the 30th, attended by Ju Zheng, Qin Zhen, Wang Yongbin, Jiao Yitang, Xie Guansheng, etc., with Ju Zheng presiding. Matters for discussion:

Unrest in French North Africa: Arabs Stirring 21

(Paris) The labor strike that has caused great damage to France in the past few days has now spread to Algeria. Four hundred indigenous workers went on strike and threw stones at the train near the Wengshi Mine today, resulting in a conflict with the gendarmerie. One indigenous person was killed. The gendarmerie has now requested assistance from the mounted police. (National telegram on the 30th)

French North Africa, Algiers, Constantine: People from both the left and right factions exchanged gunfire last night. After the police heard the news and rushed to the scene and arrested ten people, order was restored. One police officer was injured in the disturbance. Four hundred strikers at the Wunchai Iron Mine near the city opened fire on vehicles transporting ore yesterday. Two police officers escorting the road immediately returned fire and injured one worker. (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

French North Africa, Algiers, Constantine: The incident that occurred in this city and the ports of Oran and Wunchai Iron Mine yesterday has caused some anxiety throughout Algiers. However, the authorities have taken the necessary measures to prevent the situation from becoming more serious. The reason for the incident in these places is due to the dissatisfaction of the natives with the current situation. There are several reasons that can be said: Some Arabs have failed to understand European modern political theories. Since the outbreak of anti-Jewish disturbances by Palestinian Arabs, the natives here have also been stimulated. Economic depression and a large number of unemployed people. However, observers believe that no less than 10 million Arabs in Algiers have received political training and will never allow a small number of rioters to disrupt the local government. The government authorities have also taken all necessary measures to maintain law and order. (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

League of Nations Assembly Opens: Abyssinian Emperor Makes Final Effort; Fear That It Will Not Be Enough to Recover International Situation; Thorough Cancellation of Sanctions Against Italy Is Confirmed 22

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly is scheduled to hold a special meeting today to discuss the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, and is expected to focus on canceling sanctions against Italy. Before the meeting, a crowd gathered outside the door to watch the representatives arrive. The most eye-catching figure was the Emperor of Abyssinia, who drove to the League of Nations headquarters at 5 pm today. The Emperor personally led the delegation to attend the meeting and planned to appeal to the audience that Abyssinia was invaded by Italy for no reason, and that the member states of the League of Nations should continue to implement sanctions against Italy for the sake of justice. The general public believes that the Emperor's appeal may not be approved by the audience. It is an unprecedented event in the history of the League of Nations for a head of state to personally address the League of Nations Assembly. (Reuters dispatch on the 30th)

(Geneva) The extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Assembly is scheduled to open at 5 pm today. French Prime Minister Léon Blum and Foreign Minister Delbos met with Belgian Prime Minister Jilin in the morning to discuss the procedures for the meeting and reached an agreement immediately. Prime Minister Jilin will be elected as the chairman of the meeting, replacing Czech President Beneš, and will read out the note submitted by the Italian government, and then the representative of Argentina, namely the country's ambassador to Italy, Cantilo, will give a speech explaining the reasons for the country's request to convene the meeting in advance, but the representative will not submit a draft resolution to condemn Italy. The general debate will begin tomorrow, when French Prime Minister Léon Blum and British Foreign Minister Eden will deliver speeches. (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

Geneva: Dignitaries from All Countries Gather; Chairman of the Assembly Reads Italian Note; Regular Meeting in September Postponed for Ten Days 23

(Geneva) The extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Assembly is scheduled to open tomorrow afternoon. Dignitaries from all countries will gather, and there will be a lively scene with much discussion. The most eye-catching of the representatives of various countries is the Emperor of Abyssinia, who will attend in person as the head of state to advocate for Abyssinia and will request the League of Nations to provide financial assistance so that he can return to Gor, western Abyssinia, to call on his people to continue to resist the invading country. In addition, the speeches to be delivered by French Prime Minister Léon Blum and British Foreign Secretary Eden are also of great interest to the general public. The drafts of the two speeches have been prepared and will be reviewed together tonight to finalize them. Chilean representative Rivas Vicuña will then take the floor after the representatives of Britain and France to express his country's views on the issue of amending the Covenant of the League of Nations, and will request that this issue be included in the agenda of this meeting. Regarding this matter, Rivas Vicuña met with French Foreign Minister Delbos this morning to explain that he did not want to hinder the actions of the League of Nations, so if the proposed amendment to the Covenant cannot be done in fact, the wording of the Covenant may be slightly revised. Other representatives believe that the hopes of the League of Nations have been greatly shaken by the blow of the Italian-Abyssinian issue and that it is necessary to find ways to strengthen it in the future. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

(Geneva) People in the League of Nations are showing a more optimistic view of the development of the situation and the opening of the League of Nations Assembly. Belgian Prime Minister Jilin will arrive at noon tomorrow to preside over the opening of the Assembly and will submit the Italian note for reading. According to Italian sources, this note contains a compromise nature and explains that the Abyssinian government has been plotting to invade Italian territory for a year, which is the reason why Italy had to use force. During the Italian army's operations, they sought to reduce casualties as much as possible, so the result was that there was very little bloodshed and they finally conquered the entire Abyssinia. It also said that the areas occupied by the Italian army have been in a state of anarchy, with bandits rampant and the people living in misery. Italy is now going to reform them. The League of Nations will be notified of the detailed situation regarding the future administrative organization of these areas. In the past, all countries competed to engage in colonization, and all conquered and managed culturally backward areas as colonies. What Italy is doing now is the same. Moreover, from a legal point of view, the system of imitating Abyssinia is actually a voluntary trusteeship system, knowing that the responsibility is not light and the burden is heavy, but still not hesitating to accept it is nothing more than for the sake of the future of civilization. In addition, the Italian note is said to have put forward two major guarantees to the League of Nations, namely that Italy will never train native troops within the territory of the annexed land, and will only organize small police forces. In terms of economy, it will adopt the principle of open door and welcome foreign free investment. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

(Geneva) The former chairman of the League of Nations Assembly, namely Czech President Beneš, recently sent a letter to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, resigning from the position of chairman of the Assembly, saying that he was sorry for not being able to come to preside over the opening of the Assembly as the President of the Czech Republic, and that "I have always been optimistic about the future of the League of Nations. Although the League of Nations is now encountering difficulties, my views are still not affected." (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

(Geneva) Czech President Benes officially resigned from the chairmanship of the League of Nations Assembly today. At the same time, British Foreign Secretary Eden met with French Prime Minister Blanc and decided to nominate Belgian Prime Minister Jilin as the candidate chairman, and decided that if the organization of the League of Nations needs to be reformed, it should be implemented in September so that the League of Nations can be universalized within the current time and that the United States, Japan, Germany, Brazil and other countries can also participate. (National telegram on the 29th)

(Geneva) Yesterday, it was rumored here that the opening date of the League of Nations Assembly in September might be postponed to October or even later than October in order to deal with the issue after receiving Germany's reply on the Locarno issue. For a time, all parties were greatly surprised, but Britain and France claimed that the delay of the meeting by eight or ten days was only for convenience and for no other reason. (Reuters dispatch on the 30th)

(Geneva) Representatives of the Small Entente and the Balkan Entente countries hosted a banquet for Czech Foreign Minister Krofta last night and held talks. It was decided that if the Covenant of the League of Nations needs to be amended, it should be to strengthen the collective security mechanism. (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

(Geneva) Representatives of seven countries, namely Sweden, Denmark, Norway, Finland, the Netherlands, Switzerland, and Spain, who are not involved in the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, held another meeting this morning to discuss the amendment to the Covenant of the League of Nations, but no decision was made, and they agreed to consult on everything after the end of the extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Assembly. (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

Britain and France Will Not Negotiate With Italy on Abyssinia's Future System at This Time 24

(London) According to sources in Geneva, the governments of Britain and France have agreed not to negotiate with Italy on the future system of Abyssinia at this time, but to discuss it at the regular meeting of the League of Nations Assembly in September. Diplomatic circles here have expressed doubts about this news, saying that the British government has repeatedly asked the Italian government what its views are on the future system of Abyssinia. The purpose of this is nothing more than to make the country make some concessions to the League of Nations in order to resolve the issue. Italy has replied that it cannot make any concessions as long as the sanctions are not lifted. Now that there is no problem in lifting the sanctions, this issue should be considered quickly, because this issue must be resolved from the following two points of view. The two points of view are that all parties still hope that when discussing the future system of Abyssinia, the League of Nations should participate in it to some extent in order to protect part of the dignity of the League of Nations. The interests of all related countries in Abyssinia cannot be delayed. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

(London) Well-informed observers here believe today that Britain is clearly willing to cooperate with Italy again, even at the expense of Germany's friendship. Prime Minister Baldwin said in the House of Commons today that once normalcy is restored, the Admiralty has approved naval personnel of the Mediterranean Fleet to take leave. It is said that the pro-German sentiment of the British people is gradually cooling. Last week, Secretary of War Cooper's speech in Paris revealed a warning to Germany. Today, Interior Minister Simon stated that Cooper's speech did not represent the government's policy, but Germany has felt uneasy. (National telegram on the 29th)

Italian Government Submits Document to the League of Nations, Declaring Unwillingness to View Abyssinia as a Mandate Territory 25

(Geneva) Today, the Italian government will submit a memorandum to the President of the League of Nations General Assembly. The document compares Italy's current activities in Abyssinia with those carried out under the mandate system of the Treaty of Versailles. It deems the League of Nations' accusations against Italy improper and affirms Italy's intention to utilize the Abyssinian people's will. The document states that Italy will maintain an open-door policy in East Africa and is prepared to act within the League of Nations in the spirit of European cooperation, but only after the lifting of sanctions and the disbandment of self-defense groups formed as a result of the sanctions. Italy believes that genuine cooperation cannot be achieved without mutual trust. The document further declares that the rumor that Italy proposed so-called voluntary trusteeship over Abyssinia is a major misunderstanding. Italy clearly wishes to report its civilizing efforts in Abyssinia to the League of Nations, but this does not imply any form of governance. (30th, Reuters)

Italian Government Announces Demobilization of Part of the Army in Abyssinia; Small Battles Still Occurring in Various Parts of Abyssinia 26

(Rome) Today's government gazette announced that the Italian army in East Africa will undergo a large-scale demobilization. This is because the Italian army's occupation of Abyssinia was very swift, and the Abyssinian people have largely submitted. Therefore, the government will prioritize the return of the troops that were first sent to East Africa. (29th, National Telegram)

(Paris) Regarding the Italian government's decision to recall the "Gavina" Division of the army from western Abyssinia, a correspondent from "Le Petit Parisien" in Rome reported yesterday that this move is a response to the Abyssinian Emperor's statement that it is not certain whether the Italian army can conquer Abyssinia. It is also meant to demonstrate that western Abyssinia no longer requires a large army to be stationed there, and that a small number of troops performing police duties is sufficient. Italian sources believe that this move will create a good impression in Geneva. (30th, Havas)

Abyssinian Capital: An Italian army unit led by General Eloiso occupied the town of Mika near the Gambela border on June 27. This town controls the trade route from Gambela to the Abyssinian capital and Jimma and is of great military importance. The purpose of the Italian army's occupation of this town is to cut off the supply route from the Gambela side to the Abyssinians. (30th, Reuters)

(Rome) The semi-official Stefani news agency recently reported that the Italian army has occupied the Mega area on the southwestern border of Abyssinia (adjacent to British Kenya). Previously, Mega was the hub for those traveling from Kenya to Abyssinia to engage in anti-Italian propaganda. This can now be controlled. (30th, Havas)

(Rome) Today, the government allocated 1.3 billion lire for the development and colonization of Abyssinia, of which 600 million lire is for military expenses. At the same time, a telegram from the Abyssinian capital stated that an Italian army unit, heading to Mika on the border of the Galla-Sidamo colony, was attacked by Abyssinians. The Italians immediately responded with machine gun fire, causing many Abyssinian casualties. The Italian army then occupied Mika. There is also a report stating that the governors of the Sidamo and Galla provinces have expanded the Italian occupied area in the southwest and established military and civilian government organs in various places on the Kenya border. (29th, National Telegram)

(London) According to a "Daily News" correspondent in Djibouti, small-scale battles have not ceased in various places after the Italian occupation of major cities in Abyssinia. Several thousand Abyssinian fighters are also near Harar, and the Italian army has had to use aircraft to bomb them. (29th, National Telegram)

British House of Commons Meeting: Questions Arise Constantly; Citing the Statements of the Chancellor of the Exchequer and the Secretary of State for War as Pretexts to Attack the Cabinet 27

(London) The House of Commons met today, and Labour Party members, with the Speaker's permission, held an emergency debate. The debate centered on Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain's speech on June 20, which foreshadowed that Britain would advocate lifting sanctions against Italy, and Secretary of State for War Cooper's speech on June 24, which included the phrase "The French frontier is our English frontier." When Labour opposition leader Attlee began the debate, the House was full. Attlee criticized Prime Minister Baldwin's absence (the Prime Minister is resting in the countryside for several days), and then criticized the Secretary of State for War, saying that cabinet members have no right to make separate statements on major public policy matters outside of the House. He expressed his sympathy for the close friendship between Britain and France, but said that the Secretary of State for War's speech has been interpreted as an intention for Britain and France to form a close military alliance, which is contrary to the British government's policy. Baldwin should come to the House in person to announce the policy, and then cabinet members should hold their tongues. Liberal Party leader Sinclair then spoke, saying that he believed Secretary of State for War Cooper's speech was sufficient to demonstrate the government's uncertain purpose, which has reduced Britain's prestige and endangered peace. Churchill then declared that he heard that the draft of Cooper's speech had been reviewed and revised by the Foreign Secretary. He thought this was a very good speech, and its emotions were admirable. Cooper did not say a word against anyone except those countries with aggressive intentions. Home Secretary Simon, representing the government, stated the reasons for the Prime Minister's absence and denied the Secretary of State for War's claim to form a military alliance with France, saying that this kind of accusation is based on baseless words. Simon recounted the situation when the Secretary of State for War gave this speech, saying that his words were not announcing policy, but only wanted to make the people of both countries aware of the urgency of the overall situation. The place to announce policy is naturally the House of Commons, but the government's policy has already been thoroughly announced by Eden and Baldwin in the House of Commons debates on June 18 and 23. The Secretary of State for War's viewpoint is not in conflict with this declaration. The Secretary of State for War sent the draft of his speech to the Foreign Office before the speech, and the Foreign Secretary revised certain sections, but the final draft was not seen by the Foreign Secretary because he was preoccupied with other matters and did not have time to do so, but this was not intentional disregard. At this point, Conservative Party member Wilson rose to say that the speeches of the Chancellor of the Exchequer and the Secretary of State for War have caused genuine disturbance and panic among those who support the government. Simon replied that he did not think the Secretary of State for War's remarks had this effect. It should be noted that his words did not announce the government's policy. (29th, Reuters)

(London) When the House of Commons met yesterday afternoon, the opposition leaders raised questions about Secretary of State for War Duff Cooper's speech at the Anglo-French Association in Paris, but the language used was not very intense. This was due to the absence of Prime Minister Baldwin, which resulted in a loss of a target for attack. It is also a fact that the leaders' criticism of the Secretary of State for War was not as severe as their criticism of the lack of coordination among the cabinet members. The Chancellor of the Exchequer, Chamberlain, had already given a speech at the Conservative Club supporting the repeal of sanctions against Italy, and Secretary of State for War Duff Cooper had advocated Anglo-French mutual understanding in Paris. The opposition parties could not help but seize on this as a pretext to mock the cabinet, saying that the method of announcing foreign policy was so circuitous that it was ridiculous. In addition, the Secretary of State for War's speech did not mention a word about the collective security policy based on the League of Nations Covenant, which was also unsatisfactory to the opposition parties. Home Secretary Sir John Simon, representing the cabinet, replied that the Secretary of State for War's remarks were only reiterating the views previously expressed by Prime Minister Baldwin. His speech in Paris was addressed to audiences in both Britain and France, and it was necessary to emphasize the common interests of both parties, which was very moving and sufficient to convince the opposition parties. (30th, Havas)

(London) Regarding the speech given by Secretary of State for War Duff Cooper at the Anglo-French Association in Paris a few days ago, several government-affiliated members of parliament recently proposed a motion in the House of Commons, saying, "The House is confident that the government will certainly avoid providing any promises in the military or other fields that would lead the world to believe that Britain has formed an alliance treaty with France or with Soviet Russia, and hopes that it will follow the declaration made by former Prime Minister MacDonald in the House of Commons in June 1933 to promote mutual relations between Britain, France, and Germany." (30th, Havas)

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin has been resting in Cotswolds for many days. At a time when opposition members of parliament are wantonly attacking him, he has delayed his return to the capital, which has led to speculation from the outside world. Political figures believe that the Prime Minister's health is failing and that stepping down is only a matter of time. One theory is that the mention of failing health is a way to prepare for retirement. Other observers say that the Prime Minister will retire between July and August of this year. The Prime Minister originally hoped to retire after King Edward VIII's coronation ceremony in May of next year, because the King's coronation coincides with the Prime Minister's 70th birthday. Most people believe that the Prime Minister should step down before the King's coronation, but officials insist that the Prime Minister has been working very hard in recent months to handle state affairs. His trip to Cotswolds is purely due to physical reasons, and there are no other reasons. (30th, Havas)

(Berlin) After French Premier Leon Blum, Foreign Minister Delbos, and British Foreign Secretary Eden held talks in Geneva the other day, it was heard that their opinions had become consistent, and the talk of an Anglo-French alliance had become very rampant. The "Frankfurter Zeitung" recently commented on this and warned Britain, saying, "Those who advocate an Anglo-French alliance, such as the extreme Conservative member of parliament Churchill, Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, and Secretary of State for War Duff Cooper, are now making grand pronouncements. However, if Britain is drawn into this kind of alliance treaty and adopts a mechanical policy of mutual assistance obligations, it will be extremely dangerous in terms of the country's interests. This is something that Churchill and his ilk should know." (29th, Havas)

Eighteen States in the United States Experience Insect and Drought Disasters 31

Losses Exceed 100 Million Yuan

Chicago: According to a survey report released by the Associated Press today, 18 states are currently experiencing drought and insect disasters. Farmers' losses are estimated to exceed 100 million yuan. The disaster area forms a large triangle, with its edges being Ohio, the Mississippi River, Mississippi, and the Rocky Mountains. The situation in the southeastern states is said to be serious, but the recent rains have alleviated the damage somewhat. The barley region of Canada has also benefited from the rains. However, the northwestern states have become an insect world, and the desire for rain is strong. The insects are mostly grasshoppers, and the affected states include Iowa, Missouri, Nebraska, Colorado, Wyoming, and Oklahoma. It is reported that damage to clothing and equipment is also significant. Recently, rainfall in Colorado and Wyoming has only been one-third of normal, and there has been very little rainfall in the Dakotas in the past two months. In Montana, wheat stalks wither when they grow to only one foot. In most places, the grasslands have turned yellow, so livestock ranchers have had to transport their livestock elsewhere to find forage. (29th, National Telegram)

US Department of Commerce Analyzes the Chinese Economy 34

Tax-Evading Imports Reach 300 Million Yuan

Washington: The US Department of Commerce's analysis of China's 1935 international balance of payments reveals that China suffered significant losses from smuggling, with tax-evading imports reaching a massive 300 million yuan. Another 10 million yuan is said to have been used to pay for smuggled imports of gold. Smuggled exports of gold reached 20 million yuan, and smuggled exports of silver reached 150 million yuan. This shows the prevalence of tax-evading activities in China. According to the balance of payments, both receipts and payments are 1,429,000,000 yuan. Payments include imports worth 919,000,000 yuan, smuggled imports worth 300,000,000 yuan, foreign debt repayments secured with water, 66,000,000 yuan, US wheat loans 13,000,000 yuan, salt tax guarantees 12,000,000 yuan, railway income guarantees 16,000,000 yuan, totaling 107,000,000 yuan in these payments, smuggled imports of gold 10,000,000 yuan, profits earned by foreign businesses in China remitted overseas 20,000,000 yuan, expenses for Chinese embassies and consulates abroad, travel expenses abroad, and expenses for sending students abroad 10,000,000 yuan, interest on Chinese domestic debt purchased by foreigners remitted abroad 5,000,000 yuan, and the exchange stabilization fund held abroad appears to be 30,000,000 yuan. Other capital flight, foreign investment, and losses suffered on overseas speculation may also be 28,000,000 yuan. As for income, exports amount to 576,000,000 yuan, profits earned on foreign exchange from exports 87,000,000 yuan, export duties 21,000,000 yuan, gold exports officially recorded by customs 39,000,000 yuan, smuggled exports 20,000,000 yuan, silver exports officially recorded by customs 50,000,000 yuan, smuggled exports 150,000,000 yuan, remittances from overseas Chinese, from the puppet state 30,000,000 yuan, from other sources 250,000,000 yuan, totaling 550,000,000 yuan, expenses for foreigners traveling to China 7,000,000 yuan, expenses for churches and charities in China 25,000,000 yuan, expenses for foreign embassies, consulates, army and navy in China 80,000,000 yuan, income from foreign securities purchased by Chinese 5,000,000 yuan, expenses for foreign cargo ships in China 20,000,000 yuan, extension of foreign investment credit, capital inflow for speculation 60,000,000 yuan. (29th, National News Agency)

The Sasaki Murder Case: Witnesses Continued to Testify Yesterday 36

(Peiping) Mr. Kobe, the owner of a certain shop, testified yesterday that he saw a British soldier chasing a person on Hatamen Street around midnight on May 26. The British consulate continued the hearing today. Kobe was cross-examined by a lawyer, and the entire court paid close attention. Kobe confessed that every night until midnight, there are very few pedestrians on Hatamen Street, and the street lights are not bright. He confirmed that the person chasing another was indeed a British soldier. Also, Sasaki's friend, Sazuka (transliteration) was wearing yellow shorts and a blue jacket, and he naturally recognized him as the person being chased. Kobe also answered the lawyer's questions, saying that the person being chased was lost, that he had seen him at the beginning of the chase, that he did not know Sazuka, and then was asked a few more questions, but Kobe could not give a definite answer. Next, Sazuka, an employee of the "puppet state," testified that on May 26, he and Sasaki arrived in Peiping from Zhangjiakou. That evening, he, Sasaki, and another friend had dinner at the Kinazawa Coffee House on Hatamen Street and drank eight or nine quarts of beer, but Sasaki drank very little. He was not drunk. They left the restaurant after midnight, but could not remember the exact time because he was still wandering around. His friend left first, and he and Sasaki slowly walked northeast on the street and met Kobe, who asked if they had bought long-distance bus tickets to Chengde for the next morning. While they were talking, two British soldiers walked past them, wearing yellow uniforms and white belts. He was sure they were British soldiers because of their shoulder badges and military caps. The two soldiers were walking on the west side of the street, heading north. Sasaki and he then also headed north, crossing the street to the west side. While crossing the street, he saw one soldier turn around and hit a rickshaw puller. This was still the two soldiers he had seen initially. The fight started on the east side of the street, and he and Sasaki were on the west side of the street, so they stopped to watch. Then, he continued walking and urged Sasaki to follow him, saying that there was no need to waste time, but Sasaki remained standing still. Then, he heard someone running and saw a soldier running towards him. The soldier who had hit the rickshaw puller ran towards Sasaki. Fearing that he would be beaten, he ran. As the soldier was about to catch up with him, he turned around and pushed him, and the soldier lost his balance and fell to the ground. As he fled, he urged Sasaki to flee as well, but when he looked back, he saw Sasaki taking a few steps back as another soldier approached him. Then, Dr. Terada testified about the cause of Sasaki's death. He wore rubber gloves and a face mask and took Sasaki's brain from a basket to present it as evidence. The spectators were shocked. The royal lawyer, Mr. Bourke, then ordered him to put it away. Terada also said that there was also Mr. Onishi, a Japanese person, who was beaten by a British soldier in a Korean liquor stall on the same day. His injuries were the same as Sasaki's, which proved that he was hit by the same weapon. After being cross-examined, Terada replied that he thought the artery in the brain would not be indirectly vibrated and ruptured. Sazuka will continue to appear in court tomorrow morning to testify. (30th, Reuters)

Overseas Correspondence

Prospects for Buddhism in Europe 55

Opposition is one of the natural phenomena in the world. Cold and heat multiply each other, and surplus and deficit are divided, and the general rate is similar. However, the opposition between Eastern and Western cultures has gradually become an undeniable fact since the 19th century. Originally, the politics and religion of the East took peace as the central thought, and reaching Great Harmony from peace as the highest goal, while the politics and religion of the West took force as the central thought, and reaching Great Harmony from force as the highest goal. Therefore, those who cherish virtue lose their power, and each follows its own path. When the religious wars, material civilization, and aggressive policies of the West were at their peak, the religious freedom, spiritual civilization, and politeness of the East became more and more oppressed. The so-called white race is naturally arrogant. However, since the European War from 1914 to 1920, the Western powers have felt that the people's livelihood is declining and unbearable. The masses have realized the pain and thought deeply, and hesitated at the crossroads. They have gradually realized that the previous central thought of force was inappropriate, and they should strive to find a way to recover. Therefore, Eastern philosophy, Buddhism, etc., have taken the opportunity to revive and move westward. For example, the popular translations of Confucianism and Lao Tzu's theories in various countries are of course needless to say. Even the rise of Buddhist associations and widespread dissemination are enough to symbolize the changes of the times. If there is a so-called critical point in the opposition between Eastern and Western cultures, this is the time. Now, if you examine 100 Westerners, there are many who oppose aggressive wars and do not advocate rejecting foreign religions. Confucianism cherishes universal love, Buddhism takes compassion as its foundation, and Lao Tzu takes inaction as governance. The spirit of Eastern civilization is enough to fascinate Westerners. Isn't that so? The reporter is not talented and would like to briefly describe the current situation of Buddhism in Europe.

The initial step of Buddhism in Europe dates back to the end of the 19th century. According to the self-report of German Buddhist C.T. Staauss, Frankfurt am Mrin, who is 84 years old, he has been reading Edwin Arnold's Light of Asia since 1887. In 1891, the Mahabodhi Society was established in India. The 84-year-old Buddhist was a member of the Society at that time. The head of the Society, the Indian monk Anagasika Dharmapala, represented Ceylon at the World Religious Conference in Chicago, USA in 1893. The German was formally ordained by this monk.

In 1904, an Englishman named Alan Bennett, with the Dharma name Ananda Metteyya, introduced Buddhism to England from Qiu, but he died within a few years. His disciples commemorated him with the Buddhist Review, a famous Buddhist magazine in Qiu. The magazine was printed for 12 years. Later, it was suspended to transfer funds to build a Buddhist Lodge. The Buddhist Lodge was initially named Lodge of the Theosophical Society. Not long after the completion of the Lodge, the Indian monk Anagarika Dharmapala came to preach and created the Buddhist Mission 41, which is still very popular today. The Buddhist Mission also has the establishment of the Mahabodhi Society, which is now the mainstay of Buddhism in England. In September 1934, the Society convened the first European Buddhist Representative Conference, which was very grand for a time.

The British Buddhist Mahabodhi Society is located in London at 41, Gloncester Raadf Regent’s Park, Londonf N,. W.I. Its host is A.H. Perkins. It has five main purposes: To widely disseminate the Pali classics and Buddhist teachings; To practice Buddhism with integrity; To establish a Buddhist library in London; To subsidize preaching monks stationed in Europe; To contact and help other Buddhist groups in Europe. The Society has a preaching lecture once a week. The annual membership fee is six shillings, and the permanent membership fee is five pounds. The Society's publication, The Wheel, is published monthly and sells for four pence, free for members. It also publishes many books, but they are all superficial and not worth introducing. The Society also plans to recruit a minimum of 4,000 members in the shortest possible time.

In addition, there is also a Buddhist Mission in Liverpool, but the details are unknown.

The establishment of the German Buddhist Association began in 1922, with the association name Gemeinde um Audda and the address in Berlin. The founder, German Herrl Martin Steinke, has now been shaved as a monk, with the Dharma name Tao Chun. He published a magazine named Lie Brockensammlung. Later, German Dr. Paul Dahlke (deceased) founded another Buddhist temple in Berlin. The temple is a beautiful palace, and its disciples hold preaching celebrations every first and fifteenth day of the lunar month. Easterners often come to join in the fun. In the summer of 1933, Dharma Master Ananda Kansayayana preached here. The Japanese monk Junji Sukakibara once lived here for two years. Dharma Master Rehela Sankrityayana came to live for two weeks three years ago. In addition, Georg Grimm created the Lodge of Three Jewels, while in Hamburg (Hamburg - hosted by Herr Persian) and Konisburg, there is also a Buddhist association house. The exquisite Buddhist temple created by Dr. Dahlke is named Das Buddhistische Hosu, hosted by Mr. Guide Auster. The French Buddhist Society (Guide Auter Les Smis du) was founded by Dharma Master Taixu when he traveled to Europe a few years ago. The members are from France, Germany, England, the United States, Russia, Hungary, and other countries.

Switzerland also has a Buddhist association, located in Locarno, Geneva. There are many other Buddhists scattered in Italy, the Czech Republic, and major cities in Germany, which cannot be described in detail.

As for the hosts of the Buddhist Associations Bonddhisme Dharmapasa Trust in India and Ceylon, they are Daya Hewaqitarne and NID. S. Silva.

Glimpses of European Buddhist Opinions - European Buddhist opinions best represent the extent of Westerners' understanding of Buddhism and their preaching methods. In the following sections, I will translate them directly and roughly, omitting names to save space.

Modern Europe urgently needs Buddhism to liberate the mechanized life of the Western masses. Western materialism and selfishness will lead to the destruction of world culture. Only the spirit of the Buddha in heaven can save it. We, regardless of East or West, Europe or Asia, or skin color, are all believers in the light of Asia. I deeply wish to be reborn in the Buddhist land of India in the next life. Buddhism is the foundation of peace and the solvent of sin. In the future, the work of the Buddhist Association should focus on training European and Asian youth for preaching work. I hope that Buddhist organizations in the East will do their best to donate funds for preaching in the West, just as Westerners preach in the East. Some say that the East is poor and may not have the remaining power to go to the West. This is a big mistake. The West must build more temples and monasteries for Buddhist disciples to practice. In terms of the Western environment and customs, the architecture of Buddhist temples should be built in the Western style, just like Buddhist temples in China, Tibet, Ceylon, and Japan have different styles. There are two weaknesses in Western Buddhist preaching: First, talent and strength are not concentrated; second, the economy is not abundant. Magazines should also use English, French, and German to circulate in various European countries. It is very uneconomical for each country to publish separately. Apart from the Buddhist scriptures, there is no other way to bring world peace. Gathering a large number of peaceful people can create a peaceful culture. The power of monarchs, soldiers, and political and legal authorities is not as great. The power of Bolshevism, Fascist Imperialism, and Democracy is also not as great. Our summer school has been able to practice non-killing and relieve poverty. In the future, I hope that Buddhist countries in the East will generously provide assistance in order to prosper. I hope that we Europeans will not regard Buddhism as a doctrine, a theory, a philosophy, or literature, but as a way of life, so that it can be used to correct the various shortcomings of Christianity's enlightenment of the West. Christianity in Germany has reached its final stage. After that, the development of Buddhism will undoubtedly progress day by day. German Buddhists seem to be hiring a Dharma Master from the East to stay in Europe permanently to facilitate preaching. The value of a Dharma Master is far greater than that of a magazine. Buddhism is always fresh, always fashionable, always bright, and always suitable for the needs of life. We must support vegetarian associations and oppose all cruel scientific behaviors.

The reporter described the opinions of Western Buddhists, and I can't help but feel deeply. Can Buddhism really stop European materialism, aggression, and selfishness? Will the weak and small nations of the East forever rely on Buddhism to survive? Does the world really not need material civilization? Judging from the current state of the world, these issues are still just empty talk and fantasies. Western Buddhists have a shallow understanding of Buddhism and urgently need the assistance of Eastern Buddhist organizations. They also urgently need Eastern assistance in preaching expenses. Are Easterners unmoved? When will this opposition of Eastern and Western cultures be like the opposition of cold and heat in water, completely reaching uniformity? Great Harmony, Great Harmony, I look forward to it.

Japanese Are Exerting All Their Efforts to Seize the Chinese Wool Market 56

Planning to Take the American Commercial Rights into the Hands of Japan - The Current Manchurian-Mongolian Wool Company is Actively Proceeding

Shenyang News: The Manchurian-Mongolian Wool Weaving Company established by the Japanese has now increased its capital by 3 million yuan in order to be active in the markets of Northeast China, North China, and South China. It is reported that the company plans to study and improve Chinese wool, starting from practical aspects. The factories in Shenyang, Nagoya, and Okazaki, as well as the Okazaki factory, all take Chinese wool products as the principle. In the future, it plans to add a factory in Tianjin, taking that place as the center, and transfer the commercial rights of Chinese wool from the United States to Japan. Therefore, a group of investigators from the Ministry of Colonial Affairs and the Manchurian-Japanese Merino Association, who went to Tianjin a few days ago, are engaged in investigating North China wool and the progress strategy of the company, and are actively promoting its realization.

Shandong Province to Implement the Third Phase of Abolishing Illegal Taxes and Levies 57

Provincial and County Petty Taxes and Brokerage Fees to Be Completely Abolished, and Field Tax Surcharges in Various Counties to Be Reduced

Jinan Correspondence: Our province is complying with the Central Government's order to abolish illegal taxes and levies. In the past two phases, 780,000 yuan were abolished. There are still more than 400,000 yuan left, which will be completely abolished. However, the taxes and levies in various counties are mostly used for legitimate purposes. If there is no way to compensate for them, sudden abolition will inevitably hinder the progress of government affairs. Therefore, it has been delayed until now and has not been implemented. Wang Xiangrong, Director of the Finance Department, has allocated 40% of the Central Government's stamp tax to our province. The 160,000 yuan (stamp tax revenue of 800,000 yuan for the whole year) that should have been allocated from January to June of this year, which falls within the scope of the 24th year, has already been allocated for land reporting purposes. It is planned that starting from the 25th year, this fund will be used to offset the abolition of illegal taxes and levies at the provincial and county levels. Regarding this work, the Finance Department has carefully calculated that, in addition to allocating 10% of the stamp tax, 80,000 yuan, to cover the expenses of the Shandong Donation and Tax Management Committee, 12,000 yuan, the remaining amount will be used to abolish petty taxes and brokerage fees at the provincial level, and 30% of the county stamp tax revenue, 240,000 yuan. It has been found that the field tax surcharge in various counties is excessive. The number of counties with the highest field tax is 62. It is planned to issue a general order to limit the regular tax to one yuan, and the surcharge should not exceed one yuan and five jiao. The reduced amount will be offset by more than 70,000 yuan of the stamp tax revenue, and the remaining tens of thousands of yuan will be used to abolish the local illegal taxes and levies in various counties. The detailed list of illegal taxes and levies that should be imposed in each county has now been specified, and a general order has been issued to each county to implement it on July 1st. It is estimated that there are still more than 300,000 yuan of remaining taxes and levies in the province. In the next phase, they can be completely abolished.

Jiading: Tragedy Arises from Jealousy and Adultery 58

Li Axiu, a woman from Baitang Village, a commoner village in the Third District, Jiading, is 21 years old and has been betrothed to a man surnamed Li. The wedding will take place this winter. However, she is promiscuous. Two years ago, she had an affair with Xu Jinghe, who lives in Dongmaojiazhai. Now, there is Xu Taixin, who also lives in Maojiazhai. He graduated from the special training class of the county's security regiment. He recently became a widower after losing his wife. Li also developed a relationship with him. Jinghe was jealous and resentful. He repeatedly borrowed money from Taixin to cause trouble. Taixin did not succumb to him. At dusk on the 29th, Jinghe went to cause trouble again. Taixin expelled him with force. Jinghe was no match for him and returned home. He immediately took a sharp blade and went again. Taking advantage of Taixin's lack of preparation in the dark, he stabbed him seven times in a row, one in the chest and four or five in the abdomen. He died instantly. Axiu heard the sound and came out to look. She was also stabbed twice in the left waist, and then stabbed several times in a row. Her intestines flowed out of her abdomen. The murderer, having achieved his goal, went directly to the Xuhang Public Security Police Station under its jurisdiction, turned himself in, and was escorted to the county this morning by the station with a document. Li Axiu, who was injured, and Xu Weiyuan were sent to the Jiading Hospital in the city by people that night. After the doctor's treatment, Axiu would be safe if she did not develop inflammation within a day and night. However, Weiyuan's intestinal wall was ruptured, and feces flowed out. Although he was sutured, he eventually died. He died at 10 am this morning (30th). Shan Longbao, the trial officer of the county government, together with the police, has separately identified the corpses, ordered the family members of the deceased to coffin and bury them, and detained the murderer Xu Jinghe for investigation.

Suzhou: Shanghai Youth Comes to Suzhou to Commit Suicide 59

At about 7 pm the night before last (29th), a young Shanghai traveler opened room 94 at the Sanxin Hotel outside Changmen. He wrote that he was from Shanghai, named Xu Huizhong, 22 years old. After resting in the room for a while, he strolled around the various halls. Then he went out to buy things near the road. After a short stay, he returned, closed the door, and went to sleep. At about 2 am yesterday morning, the tea boy on duty suddenly heard groans in the room. He hurriedly opened the door and entered, only to see that Xu's face was pale, his mind was confused, and there were bright red bloodstains on his lips. An empty bottle of Lysol water was also found upstairs. Knowing that he had taken Lysol and committed suicide, he was rushed to Suyong Hospital for treatment. He improved slightly, but the poisoning was too deep, and his life was no longer guaranteed.

The Suzhou-Jiading Highway Is Transferred to Commercial Operation 60

The Suzhou-Jiading Highway long-distance bus was formerly operated by the Jiangsu Construction Department Highway Management Office. Three years have passed since it opened to traffic. Now, Chen Qinshi, a celebrity from Wuxing, has negotiated with the construction departments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to change it to commercial operation, which will be implemented starting today (July 1st). Mr. Chen came to Suzhou on the afternoon of the 30th to handle the handover matters. After the road is transferred to commercial operation, the car price will be appropriately reduced to two cents per kilometer. All ten vehicles have been transported to Suzhou on the 30th. The old vehicles will be transported to Jiangbei by the Jiangsu Construction Department for application. The commercial operation period is 20 years, and a deposit of 5,000 yuan will be paid first. Zheng Rong, the new vehicle affairs chief, came to Suzhou and inspected the road to Jiaxing on the 30th. It is heard that the staff at each station will generally not be changed in order to ensure skilled personnel.

Wujiang Air Defense Drill in Urban Area 62

Yesterday (29th) afternoon from 6:00 PM to 9:00 PM, an air defense drill was held in the urban area of this county. The Public Security Bureau prepared for it in advance. At 6:30 PM, the first alarm sounded, and all traffic in the city was cut off. At the second alarm, the fire brigades went to the front of the County Temple to extinguish the simulated fires caused by bomb explosions. They quickly extinguished the fires. During the emergency, the detectives of the Public Security Bureau, acting as rioters, staged a simulated robbery in the bustling area of North Pond Street. The Public Security Bureau opened fire and captured them, creating a lifelike scene. At 8:15 PM, another emergency alarm sounded, and all shops in the city closed and turned off their lights. Pedestrians were not allowed on the streets until martial law was lifted at 9:00 PM.

Wuxi Young Woman Commits Suicide Due to Quarrel 64

Zhao Maoxiu, a resident of No. 34, Housimen Street, Tuiguan Arch, in the city, is 32 years old. He used to work at a money house in Shanghai. In the 20th year of the Republic, he married Wang Shiqin, the daughter of Wang Chuanlu from Xiaoheshang, as his wife. They have one son and one daughter. Recently, Zhao lost his job and returned home. His relationship with his wife Shiqin became strained, and he stayed at his mother's brother's home for recuperation. The day before yesterday afternoon, Maoxiu returned home, and the couple suddenly had a quarrel. Overwhelmed with anger, he attempted suicide. However, his family members persuaded him to stop. Afterwards, Wang was also depressed. Yesterday (30th) morning, at about 3:00 AM, Wang secretly took poison in her room. Her family members noticed and rushed her to Puren Hospital for treatment. However, she had taken too much poison, and it was too late. She eventually died, causing much discussion among the nearby residents. The reason for Wang's poisoning is even more difficult to guess. Also, Zhang Rulin, a Changshu traveler at the Jiaotong Hostel under the Gongyun Bridge, also committed suicide due to economic pressure.

Reorganizing Shantytowns in the Urban Area 65

The county government of this county believes that there are many shantytowns scattered throughout the urban area, making management difficult. In order to reorganize them, a Reorganization Committee for Shantytowns in the Urban Area has been specially established. In addition to the heads of various agencies and organizations such as the Party Headquarters, County Government, Construction Bureau, Education Bureau, Public Security Bureau, Land Bureau, First District Office, Rickshaw Trade Association, and Rickshaw Pullers Association serving as ex officio members, Qian Sunqing and Xue Mingjian have also been invited to serve as members. County Magistrate Long Tiyao has been designated as the permanent committee member. The committee has established seven sections: General Affairs, Investigation, Construction, Implementation, Education, Sanitation, and Design. Yesterday, County Magistrate Long convened the first preparatory meeting, which passed the draft organizational regulations for the Reorganization Committee for Shantytowns in the Urban Area and the general outline of the plan for reorganizing shantytowns in the urban area. It was also decided to conduct a trial in the First District first, with the Investigation Section conducting a preliminary survey of locations. It was also stipulated that the urban shantytown area should be limited to a maximum of ten districts. All shantytown residents should move into the districts within six months. Each shantytown district should have at least one elementary school, one literacy school for civilians, and a public hall and entertainment venue. The funds will be subsidized by deductions from the rickshaw rental fees collected by each rickshaw company.

Changshu County Middle School Principal Accused 66

The County Middle School here is the highest institution of learning in the county, and the selection of the principal is a matter of great importance to all parties. Recently, during the school's graduation examination, the Education Department sent Zhou Bowen to Changshu to conduct spot checks. It was discovered that the students had formed small groups and were distributed throughout the classrooms. Excellent students were assigned to the students in front, behind, left, and right as "central distributors." During the arithmetic spot check, Commissioner Zhou discovered the scheme on the spot and suspended all testing, pending reporting to the Education Department for review. Commissioner Zhou believed that this type of organized cheating was clearly pre-planned and expressed his dissatisfaction. Now, citizens such as Zhao Shijie have filed a petition with the Education Department, stating that this situation was caused by the principal Gu Yanru's usual negligence and requesting his replacement. There are many individuals actively seeking to succeed him, including Zhu Yinli and Zhang Yuanming.

Military Training Begins 67

Military training here began today (July 1st). It is being conducted first in the urban and suburban First District. The rural areas are being postponed due to the busy farming season. The First District has selected 1,080 conscripts ranging in age from 20 to 30. On the first day, they gathered at the Public Gymnasium to form teams. Afterwards, they were divided into three training locations: Xueqian Elementary School, Taqian Elementary School, and Sangyuan Field. The training time is from 6:30 AM to 8:00 AM every day. Patrol officers, patrol sergeants, and squad leaders from the security team are serving as trainers. The participation rate has been exceptionally high, with both wealthy and working-class individuals enthusiastically joining.

Yangzhou Elderly Woman Killed by Lightning 68

Chen, the mother of Qiu Hengliang, a farmer from Qiujiagang Village, Hangjiaji Township, Third District of Jiangdu County, was over 80 years old and blind. Yesterday (28th) afternoon, Hengliang went out, and Chen was sitting idle at home with her twelve-year-old granddaughter, Xiaogaizi, and another neighbor girl. At about 3:00 PM, the sky suddenly changed, with black clouds spreading everywhere. Heavy rain poured down, and lightning struck suddenly. A thunderous sound shook the area. When Hengliang and others returned after the rain, they found Chen and Xiaogaizi killed by lightning in the room. The neighbor girl was lying unconscious in the courtyard, soaked in the rain. They felt her chest and found it was still warm. After feeding her ginger soup, she gradually recovered. When asked about what happened, she said that when the thunder sounded, a flash of lightning entered the house first, knocking her out into the courtyard. She was still conscious at that time. Then, a thunderous sound shocked her, and she lost consciousness.

Qingjiang Execution by Shooting for Opposing Land Survey and Conscripted Labor 69

Feng Yucai, a resident of Peihui Township, Siyang County, had incited over a thousand villagers to oppose the land survey, destroyed instruments, and killed surveyors in the autumn of the previous year. At the same time, he used the villagers' opposition to the Huai River project conscripted labor, destroyed the District Office, and resisted government troops, causing social unrest. Fortunately, the provincial and county troops were able to quell the unrest. However, the suspect remained at large after the incident. The Xin Jiangtian steamer, which travels between Shanghai and Ningbo, departed from Shanghai for Ningbo on the 27th. Unexpectedly, when the ship reached the waters off Litongsha, he jumped into the sea and committed suicide. At that time, the other passengers and the tea server were unaware. Xiangshan's Richest Man Robbed by Bandits 71

He Minqiu, the owner of He Gongfang in Xixiang, Xiangshan, is the richest man in the county. He has more than ten guards at home for protection. Unexpectedly, at midnight on the 25th, five bandits, each wielding weapons, entered the house by scaling the wall from the backyard. Letter 73

To the esteemed editor:

I was deeply surprised to read the news item "Severe Urging of Old Taxes" from Jiaxing in your newspaper's third page on June 26th. After investigation, our county is handling all procedures for summoning and detaining tax-delinquent property owners in accordance with regulations in this tax collection effort. We are especially strict in restraining the collection police. All detained people are delinquent taxpayers, and there have been no cases of suicide. The original news report, which stated that "there have been many cases of suicide due to fear of the harshness of the tax police and inability to pay," is entirely fabricated, with no factual basis. As for the provincial officials led by Wei Songtang, who were recently sent to Jiaxing, they came specifically to investigate land tax and deed tax matters. The original news report, which stated that "the people are already impoverished, and the province, upon learning of this, has sent Wei Songtang and others to Jiaxing to investigate the rural situation in order to verify the facts," is even more untrue. I am concerned that this will obscure the truth and mislead the public, so I am writing to request that your newspaper promptly correct this information to avoid misunderstandings. With best wishes,

The Secretariat of the Jiaxing County Government, June 27th.

Three Special Trains Transported Antiquities Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 74

A total of 84 boxes. Heavy guard at the North Station. All transported to the antiquities warehouse on Catholic Church Street for storage.

The antiquities from China's participation in the London Art Exhibition have returned to the country and were transported to Nanjing for exhibition. The exhibition has already closed. Among them, two boxes from the Academia Sinica, four boxes from the Henan Museum, and two boxes from the Anhui Library were taken away separately by the respective institutions in Nanjing. The remaining 84 boxes of antiquities from the Palace Museum, the Antiquities Exhibition Hall, and the private collection of Zhang Shuxun were loaded onto three special trains and transported to Shanghai on the evening of the 29th on the Beijing-Shanghai night express train. Accompanying the train were ten people, including Zhang Ouyang Banghua from the Shanghai Office of the Palace Museum, and a squad of military police. The train arrived at the North Station at 7:20 AM yesterday morning. The Public Security Bureau and the Security Corps dispatched armed police and guards to guard the platform inside and outside the North Station in cooperation with the station police. Except for two boxes of private antiquities, which were picked up by their owners, the remaining 82 boxes were transferred to several large trucks of the China Transportation Company and transported to the temporary antiquities warehouse on Catholic Church Street in the French Concession at about 8:00 AM for storage. The French Concession patrol police also dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to guard the warehouse and protect the antiquities. Under the guidance of Ouyang Banghua, the staff carefully placed the antiquities in the warehouse. The work was completed at about 12:00 PM.

Banks Investing in Rural Areas 81

Approximately 15 million yuan this year.

According to the Central News Agency, rural lending is now an important business for domestic banks. According to financial circles, this type of lending has only been conducted for three years. Initially, only the Farmers Bank of China paid attention to this. Later, the Shanghai Bank achieved considerable success in the production and sales lending for Shaanxi cotton. As a result, various banks competed to emulate this. Since the government implemented the legal tender policy last year, the financial situation has improved. However, due to the stagnation of real estate and the reform of public bonds, capital has accumulated in cities, resulting in a surplus. In order to fully utilize their capital, banks have sought to develop their business, and lending to rural areas has become their main avenue. In the future, investment in rural areas will see a significant increase. However, reviewing past performance, the most difficult issues in failing to make lending widespread and deep are the lack of talent and the disunity of organizations. These issues should be improved by banks and the government in the future. Other issues include the tendency for investment to be concentrated in prosperous areas, while poor and remote areas are still not benefiting. There must be comprehensive planning in terms of distribution. It is heard that the total amount of rural lending this year will be approximately 15 million yuan, including approximately one million yuan from the Bank of China, two million yuan from the Bank of Communications, 1.5 million yuan from the Shanghai Bank, and one million yuan from the Jin City Bank. This does not include the Farmers Bank of China, the Jiangsu Farmers Bank, and the China Agricultural Credit Syndicate. The investment areas are mainly in Anhui and Shaanxi provinces.

Yesterday Was the Semiannual Settlement Period for Banks 86

Busy for Banks and Financial Institutions. Closed Today and Tomorrow for Internal Business

Yesterday was the semiannual settlement period for banks for the first half of the 1925th year of the Republic. Banks and financial institutions were busy with settlements. In order to handle the settlements, banks, while their business hours for the public remained the same, had extended hours for internal operations. Some had extended their hours until one or two o'clock the next morning, depending on the business situation of each bank. Today and tomorrow are bank holidays for handling settlements, but internal business will continue as usual. All credit transactions and overdrafts between industry and commerce and banks had to be settled by yesterday, allowing only deposits and not debts, unless otherwise specially permitted. The police authorities in the Chinese and French concessions, in order to protect banks handling settlements and commercial and industrial settlements, specially increased the number of detectives in the bank area to strictly prevent crime. As for the profits of various banks, the Bank Association will announce them after July 2nd. The numbers circulating outside are only general speculations.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company State-Run Dock and Warehouse Management Office Established Today 91

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's docks and warehouses are located throughout various ports across the country, all in strategically important locations. The majority of these are self-operated warehouses, dedicated to the berthing of the company's ships and the loading, unloading, and storage of goods. In Shanghai, in addition to the South Warehouse (Jinliyuan) and the New Warehouse (Yangjiadu), which are self-operated, there are also the Central, North, and Hua Warehouses, which are operated for business purposes and are highly trusted by various shipping companies and merchants, enjoying thriving business. However, the original organization was not yet fully sound, resulting in a lack of complete unification of exclusive authority and insufficient strictness in management. Acting Minister Yu of the Ministry of Transportation, recognizing this issue during his inspection in Shanghai in May of this year, decided to establish a Dock and Warehouse Management Office, directly under the General Office, to oversee all warehouses and docks across the board. The aim is to unify management and command, strengthen the organization, adopt scientific management in a suitable environment, reduce turnover, and improve operational efficiency. Externally, the emphasis is on minimizing procedures for customers and facilitating convenient communication, with the goal of providing thorough service. It is believed that once customers are satisfied and the company earns a good reputation, business will undoubtedly improve, benefiting not only the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company but also the general dockworkers who depend on it for their livelihood, allowing them to increase their income. It is also rumored that the Shanghai Municipal Government is currently planning to install truck ferries, which will immediately increase the value of warehouses in Pudong, further facilitating the loading and unloading of goods. The Management Office has now been organized, with its address located next to the General Office at 33 Fuzhou Road, and is officially established today. The original management offices of the three warehouses will be simultaneously abolished and incorporated into the Dock and Warehouse Management Office. The Ministry of Transportation has appointed Tan Boying, Deputy Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, as the concurrent Manager of the Dock and Warehouse Management Office. Two assistant managers have also been appointed, one of whom is Mr. Price (Capt. G.H. Price) from the Maritime Affairs Section of the Navigation Administration Department of the Ministry of Transportation. The Ministry of Transportation has also dispatched Wu Yu, Director of the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau, to administer the oath. It is said that the ceremony will be simple, and the office will officially commence operations today.

High Price of Party and National Flags Sparks Repercussions 93

Citizens' Association Sends Letter to General Association to Evaluate Prices, Submitting Request to Central Government for Approval to Reduce Prices to Facilitate Universal Promotion

The 46th Branch of the First Special District Citizens' United Association of Shanghai believes that the high price of standard Party and National flags makes promotion difficult. It previously requested the General Association to send a letter to the General Bureau for the Production and Sale of Party and National Flags, asking for a reasonable reduction to facilitate promotion. The Bureau replied that it had no authority to set prices. The Association believes that the excessive price not only hinders promotion but also places a burden on citizens. Therefore, it sent another letter to the General Association yesterday, requesting it to evaluate an appropriate price and submit a detailed report to the central government for approval to reduce prices in order to facilitate promotion and enhance national prestige. The original letter stated: “Upon receiving your letter, we found the General Bureau for the Production and Sale of Party and National Flags' response to be official and pompous. They stated that our 46th Branch did not investigate the facts, relied on likes and dislikes, and took advantage of the situation to recklessly attack, which is displeasing to read. The high price of the flags is related to promotion. If one only seeks one's own benefit and disregards the pain of purchasing at high prices, promotion will be impossible. Because we believe the high price is a fact, we dare not remain silent, making it difficult to promote the dignified national emblem. Therefore, we must come forward to advocate for a price reduction, which is fair and just, and has nothing to do with 'relying on likes and dislikes, taking advantage of the situation, or recklessly attacking.' Since the Bureau has no authority to set prices, we can ignore it. We urge your association to first evaluate an appropriate price and submit a detailed report to Party and government agencies, which will be forwarded to the central government for approval to reduce prices. This is to emphasize uniform standards for the production and sale of the national emblem, to enhance prestige, and we will never rely on approved terms to seek profit. Our repercussions are out of love and are not unique to our organization.”

Money Exchanges Begin Abolishing "Spot Exchange Fund" Yesterday 96

Money Shops to Return Custodianship of Spot Exchange Fund, Clearing Members' Spot Exchange Balances Daily

The Shanghai Money Exchange Clearing Association, located within the Ningbo Road Guild Hall, includes both North and South Shanghai exchange money shops as members. For silver dollar transactions between members exceeding 500 yuan, official forms are required. For transactions below 500 yuan, before the end of 1924, immediate cash settlement was required. However, after the Yongfeng Bank's silver transport was robbed, the association devised a new method, requiring each member and "Yuan" small trade to deposit 10,000 taels of silver in cash with the association, which would then deposit it in Chinese and foreign banks as a "spot exchange fund" for security. After that, for outstanding amounts less than 500 yuan, only the counterpart's stamp was required, and no further cash settlement was needed, simplifying the procedure. Unexpectedly, at the end of 1926, the Yanfeng Bank declared bankruptcy, impacting the spot exchange cash of various shops, exceeding the original fund. The annual money exchange meeting in 1927 proposed and resolved that outstanding amounts would still be recorded and not settled in cash, but on the 2nd and 16th of each month, cash settlement was required to prevent the accumulation of large amounts that exceeded the 10,000 tael fund's protection. The fund was subsequently increased twice to 30,000 yuan per shop, and settlement was changed to once a year at the end of the year, under the management of the Money Exchange Joint Reserve. Following the passage of the third session's ninth regular members' meeting of the Money Exchange Association to abolish the spot exchange fund, it was implemented yesterday. The Money Exchange Reserve has returned the spot exchange funds of 30,000 yuan per shop to the 48 member shops, including Fuyuan, Hengxun, and Tongyu, transferring it into the accounts under each shop's name. From now on, members' spot exchange will be cleared with the Reserve daily. The association's announcement is recorded below: "Greetings, with reference to the proposal approved at today's ninth regular members' representative meeting, approving the third session's seventeenth executive committee's proposal to abolish the spot exchange fund of 30,000 yuan per shop deposited by members, and to return it, with all members' spot exchange to be cleared with the Reserve daily, a resolution has been passed. It was further proposed to the meeting for public decision, and the meeting resolved that transactions over 500 yuan should still use official forms sent to the association's official form office, while transactions under 500 yuan should be cleared mutually, with small official forms sent to the Reserve for daily clearing, and it was decided to implement this from June 30th. All receipts for spot exchange funds held by the various shops should also be sent to the Reserve on the 30th for transfer." The Shanghai Money Exchange Association.
