Ruan Jinji Sues News Branch Director Liao Jiongran and Others; Declared Not Guilty 100

Liao Jiongran, Director of the News Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, bureau member Huang Feiren, patrol officer Long Jianpo, and others were recently sued by Ruan Jinji, a Funing native residing on Haichang Road and engaged in construction, through attorneys Zhang Yongji and Sun Fucheng, in the District Court for dereliction of duty, infringement of freedom, fraud, and other charges. During the court hearing presided over by Judge Zhang Peiming, the plaintiff claimed that he collected rent from Tang Xiaozhang, a resident of a shantytown, but was beaten instead. He reported the incident to the police, who detained Tang Xiaozhang, but instead designated the plaintiff as the defendant and sent him to the prosecutor's office. After investigation by Prosecutor Kong, Tang was released on bail and prosecuted for assault, while the plaintiff was released. The reason for the bureau's reversal of right and wrong was that Patrol Officer Long solicited a bribe from the plaintiff without success and made false statements to Director Liao Jiongran. Bureau member Huang Feiren, without investigating the case, reversed the facts, releasing the guilty and detaining the innocent. Such darkness cannot be allowed to continue, and he requested legal action. Liao Jiongran, Huang Feiren, Long Jianpo, and others, represented by attorney Zhan Jifeng, defended in court, stating that on June 10th, the case was brought to the bureau by a patrolman from the Haichang Road post. Under interrogation, Tang Xiaozhang testified that Ruan Jinji wanted to burn down the shantytown due to a grudge. Tang heard about this, argued with Ruan, and called the police. Ruan testified that he was collecting rent from Tang, who refused to pay and threatened violence. Each side presented their own version of events, so they were both sent to the third section of the General Bureau for verification. Because arson was alleged in the mutual accusations, which is a serious offense, they should be investigated together. This was done in accordance with police regulations and is not illegal. The plaintiff is clearly pursuing a private agenda, making false accusations. At this point, the judge declared the debate closed and announced the verdict in court: the defendants were all found not guilty.

Gao Jingmei Appeals Case Against Xi Jingyong 101

Debate Concluded; Sentencing Scheduled

Xi Jingyong, a local resident, 30 years old, residing at No. 77 Ningguo An Road, Beichuan Fourth Road, is an accountant at the Accounting Office of the China Merchants Bureau, stationed at the North Station Branch. Last month, Xi was suddenly sued by Gao Jingmei, a local woman residing at No. 9 Yongping Lane, Ningbo Road, in the First Special District Court for offenses against public morals and abandonment of contract, with an attached civil suit seeking damages for loans and alimony totaling 1,650 yuan. It was alleged that three years ago, when Gao Jingmei worked as a dancer at the LaFayette Dance Hall, she met Xi, who frequented the dance hall. At that time, the defendant used sweet words and false pretenses, claiming that he had no wife and was willing to marry Gao. He promised to hold a wedding as soon as the opportunity arose. Gao Jingmei, being weak-willed, complied with his requests and was soon forced to cohabit. Later, when Gao repeatedly urged him to hold the wedding, Xi kept delaying. When he could no longer avoid it, he claimed that he already had a wife and that holding another wedding would constitute bigamy. He asked Gao Jingmei to understand his difficult situation and remain patient, with Xi providing a monthly living allowance of 100 yuan while still cohabiting. He promised to divorce his previous wife within three years and then marry Gao, and if Xi breached the contract, he would pay 5,000 dollars as alimony to Gao. A written agreement was signed on the spot and given to Gao Jingmei for safekeeping. As a result, Gao was deeply convinced. Unexpectedly, starting in February or March of last year, Xi suddenly stopped visiting. Despite various attempts to inquire, he ignored her completely and even claimed that the aforementioned document was forged by Gao. Gao Jingmei finally realized that Xi had lost his conscience and had abandoned her. She was forced to hire a lawyer and file a lawsuit. After several trials in the First Special District Court, the plaintiff's evidence was deemed insufficient and the case was dismissed. However, Gao Jingmei believed that the defendant's guilt was undeniable and, based on Article 491, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, supplemented her reasoning and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. The court approved the appeal and held a hearing yesterday. The plaintiff and defendant, each accompanied by their lawyers, arrived in court on time. The appellant first stated the reasons for disagreeing with the original judgment, and then questioned the circumstances of their meeting. Xi denied cohabiting with Gao Jingmei and issuing the written agreement. The presiding judge, believing that the case was clear, ordered the start of the debate. After the lawyers on both sides debated, he announced the conclusion and scheduled sentencing.

Lou Bing'ao Sues Traditional Chinese Medicine Practitioner for Incorrect Medication After Son's Death 102

Yu Zanchen Counters with Ancient Texts; Judge Awaits Expert Assessment

Lou Bing'ao, a Shaoxing native, runs the Lou Xingheng Clothing Store at No. 107 Peide Lane, Da Ma Road. Recently, he hired attorney Shen Xingxia and filed a criminal lawsuit in the First Special District Court against Yu Zanchen, a Yuyao native who runs the Huijiuxi Hall of Traditional Chinese Medicine, located at No. 317 Shanhai Road, for causing death by negligence. The factual basis of the lawsuit is as follows: the plaintiff's seven-year-old only son, Shuigen, developed a fever and rash on May 6th of this year. The plaintiff sought treatment from the defendant, Yu Zanchen, who prescribed medicine without taking a pulse or recording a case history. He was re-examined the following day, and the condition remained the same. Over the next five days, he was seen daily, and the prescriptions given were all without pulse readings. On the 10th, the defendant saw that the rash had turned inward and the illness had become severe. Only then did he record a pulse reading. By the 13th, the condition had become even more dangerous, so another traditional Chinese medicine practitioner, Ding Zhongliang, was called in for treatment. He determined that the defendant's diagnosis was incorrect and could not be treated. Although he tried his best to save the child, it was ineffective, and he died on the 17th. An internal attack of the rash should be treated with dispersal and support, but the defendant used 3 qian of stir-fried mulberry bark, which is a medicine that drains the lungs, causing the lung qi to weaken further. The defendant has committed a crime under Article 276, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law and should be punished according to the law. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Tan Xinzhen of the First Special District Court opened the hearing. Yu Zanchen arrived in court with his lawyer. Lou Bing'ao first stated the circumstances, and when questioned, Yu Zanchen stated that he has been practicing medicine for over ten years, is a member of the Shenzhou Medical Association, and a registered doctor with the Municipal Health Bureau. He denied the plaintiff's accusation that the use of stir-fried mulberry bark was an error and presented several medical books to prove it. Judge Tan stated that the case should be assessed by experts before proceeding. The plaintiff's lawyer argued that since the defendant is a member of the Shenzhou Medical Association, the assessment of the case should be sent to the Shanghai Traditional Chinese Medicine Association for fairness. The defendant's lawyer stated that the Shenzhou Medical Association and the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association have had disagreements, and the defendant is not a member of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association. For a fair judgment, it should be sent to an impartial body. The plaintiff's lawyer then proposed the Shanghai Branch of the Central National Medical Institute, stating that it is the highest authority on traditional Chinese medicine and would be impartial. Judge Tan agreed and ordered the case to be rescheduled.

French Concession police detective Sun Qiwan shot and killed Ji Shilin, who was injured. Subsequently, Ji A'er was detained by the police and sentenced to 20 days of detention by the court. Committee members Tong Lizhang, Ye Ruizhai, Zheng Ziliang, Sun Ruiting, Zhang Youmin, Xia Shanxiao, Sun Shengchang, Cheng Yueting (representing Tong Lizhang), He Yaozhang, and more than 30 representatives from the Nantong Association, including Ge Futian, were present. Ye Ruizhai was publicly elected as chairman. After the formalities, the chairman delivered a report.

Chairman's Report

The report stated that regarding the case of French police detective Sun Qiwan fatally shooting citizen Ji Shilin, the committee members Ye Ruizhai and Tong Lizhang investigated the truth. On June 4th, Ji A'er went to the Yue family on Runde South Lane and encountered Chen Xiangrong. Initially, they talked, but then they argued and fought. As a result, both parties agreed to meet at the Yihe Teahouse on Huanghe Road at 3 PM on June 5th for tea and mediation. Ji A'er's brother, Shilin, fearing that his brother would be at a disadvantage, went to the teahouse with him. When they arrived at the teahouse, Wu Cao Shi and others were already there. Subsequently, detective number 76 from the police station came up and asked who "Little Chongming" was (referring to Ji A'er). After asking, he pulled out handcuffs, intending to handcuff Ji A'er. At this time, his brother, Shilin, seeing the detective arresting his brother without reason, stepped forward to question him. Ji A'er, sensing that the situation was not good, and his brother went downstairs to escape. Seeing the Jis escaping, the detective chased them downstairs. He tripped and fell on the stairs, becoming enraged. He then fired a shot from his pistol, hitting Ji Shilin in the back and exiting through his chest. The deceased ran to the entrance of number 8 Jialele Road, where he collapsed and died, and so on.

Compatriot Report

Following this, the Nantong Compatriot Association representative, Ge Futian, reported the investigation of the incident, noting two suspicious points: The Chinese detective initially claimed self-defense in court, then said it was an accidental discharge. The police had sent people to mediate, but the association refused. He also requested the assistance of the association to uphold justice and expressed his gratitude, and so on.

Motions Passed

The association will first send letters to the French Police Department and the Second Special District Local Court, demanding the swift dismissal and investigation of the perpetrator, Chinese detective Sun Qiwan, and initiating a public prosecution. Demand that the French authorities effectively guarantee the safety of citizens within the concession and guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future. Send letters to the Lawyers Association's Wrongful Imprisonment Compensation Committee and the People's Legal Aid Society, requesting them to uphold justice and provide unified assistance. Organize a legal research group, inviting various legal experts to jointly research and contribute opinions for reference. Send separate letters to the district branches, requesting unified assistance in this case. Send a letter to the Second Special District Citizens' General Association, discussing effective measures to guarantee the safety of citizens in the future. Send a letter to the French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association, urging them to lodge a serious representation to ensure the safety of taxpaying citizens. Regarding private prosecution, the bereaved family will independently engage a lawyer to prosecute. Send a letter to lawyer Cai Xiaobai, thanking him for providing free legal defense, upholding justice, and expressing gratitude. Seek participation from various groups to organize the Ji Shilin Support Association to mount a comprehensive response. The Bai'er Road Shou Tang, Xiang Chun Qing Yu Tang, Lafayette Road Cai Zhi Tang, Gao Chang, and Mintini Road Xiang Shan Tang, and other Chinese medicine shops, have requested representations to cancel the French Municipal Council's Public Works Bureau's collection of pharmaceutical business license fees. (Resolved) Request the Taxpayers Association to negotiate. The current free medicine clinic should be organized and opened regularly to benefit the common people. (Resolved) Follow last year's procedure. The meeting adjourned after the discussions. It was also reported that the Second Special District Citizens' Association's Executive and Supervisory Committee will present the Ji Shilin case for discussion today.

Newly Established Creative Dog Grooming Company 105

Recently, dog grooming companies have appeared in Shanghai, one on Yidingpan Road and one on Lafayette Road. These companies are both established by foreigners, specializing in grooming and shaving the fur of dogs of all social classes, both Chinese and foreign. As the weather is getting hotter, it is essential to cut the fur on dogs' bodies to alleviate the heat. This service is similar to a person going to a barbershop, offering various styles. The highest price per session is five yuan, followed by four yuan, three yuan, two yuan, and the lowest is one and a half yuan. The shaving takes about twenty minutes using clippers, and the dogs do not experience any pain. According to people in the industry, dogs need to be groomed at least once every three months for cleanliness, and even more frequently during the summer. Recently, this new industry has been welcomed by dogs of all social classes, who are flocking there for grooming.

Two Epidemic Hospitals Open Today 108

Due to the Increasing Heat in Shanghai

Summer Epidemics Suddenly Break Out

With the increasing heat in Shanghai, summer epidemics such as gastroenteritis and dysentery have suddenly broken out. Therefore, the epidemic hospitals have opened one after another. It is learned that the First Aid Epidemic Hospital at 240 North Xizang Road and the Shanghai Epidemic Hospital at 25 Xizang Road are scheduled to open at 9 AM today to admit patients. Day and night consultations will be available. Their opening announcements are recorded below:

First Aid Epidemic Hospital

The epidemic department of this hospital will open on July 1st, providing day and night consultations, specializing in the treatment of cholera, acute gastroenteritis, dysentery, heatstroke, and other conditions (including vomiting, intestinal cramps, etc.). Hospital cars are available day and night to transport patients free of charge. The outpatient department of this hospital will open on July 1st, providing comprehensive internal and external medicine consultations free of charge. Hours are from 9 AM to 11 AM, closed on Sundays and public holidays. This announcement.

Shanghai Epidemic Hospital

This hospital will officially open its epidemic consultation department on July 1st, specializing in the treatment of cholera, vomiting, diarrhea, abdominal pain, cramps, and other epidemic diseases. Treatment and medication will be provided upon arrival, day and night, free of charge. Hospital cars are available to transport seriously ill patients. Hospital telephone number is 92412, address 25 Xizang Road, opposite the Great World.

15th Hygiene Movement Concluded Yesterday 112

Various Conference Affairs Have Begun to Conclude

The Shanghai 15th Hygiene Movement, since its opening at the People's Education Center on June 15th, has held a series of hygiene exhibitions, children's, women's and infant's, and summer hygiene guidance center activities. The Youth Service Corps, Security Corps, Security Team, police officers, hygiene inspectors, and street sweepers have carried out citywide cleaning campaigns, labor services, public place hygiene inspections, and the hygiene offices have held public place hygiene knowledge training. All of these have been completed one after another, and the conference officially closed at 10 AM yesterday at the venue according to the original schedule. The details are recorded below:

Closing Ceremony

Yesterday's closing ceremony was simple. Conference President Li Ting'an and Preparatory Committee Chairman Shen Hao were unable to attend due to official business. The conference was presided over by General Secretary Zhu Jiarang. Representatives from various organizations and groups, including Jiang Hao, Yuan Liangzhou, Yu Da, Chen Tiesheng, Zhang Shousong, Wu Zhongyao, and Shen Qifeng, and approximately 300 members of the public were present. The order was as follows: Opening, singing the Party song, paying the highest respects to the Party, National Flag, and the portrait of the Premier, the Chairman respectfully reading the Premier's will, a moment of silence, the Chairman's report, speeches, and adjournment.

Chairman's Report

The Chairman delivered the closing remarks and reported on the conference's progress, stating that this conference was jointly organized by 42 public and private organizations and groups, including the Municipal Health Bureau, New Life Movement Promotion Association, and the Public Concession Health Department. It began on the 15th and today is the last day, marking its official conclusion. This conference was larger in scale and involved more work than previous sessions. Its central focus was determined to be five areas: Children's hygiene, women's and infant's hygiene, summer hygiene, public place hygiene, and labor services. Various activities were carried out based on these areas. In terms of publicity, there were two types of slogans: color-printed tin and paper. Publications included a special hygiene issue and a summary of summer hygiene, totaling 110,000 copies. Daily special issues were published in newspapers, and speeches were given by celebrities and experts on the China West Gospel City Council radio stations. In terms of exhibitions, four organizations participated, including the Ministry of Health, the Central Factory Inspection Office, the Health Bureau, and the Public Concession Health Department, displaying over 5,000 charts and models. The venue's central activities were scheduled for one type each day, with various participating organizations and groups taking responsibility, providing much guidance on children's and women's and infant's hygiene. It is estimated that over 10,000 people visited the venue each day, a thriving situation. In terms of promotion, the Security Committee, Public Security Bureau, Security Corps, Health Bureau, and New Life Movement Youth Service Corps sent over 5,000 people to carry out cleaning campaigns, labor services, and public place hygiene inspections, all of which were very effective. In summary, although this conference has come to a successful conclusion today, the enthusiastic assistance of public and private organizations, groups, individuals, and the press should be acknowledged and thanked on behalf of the conference.

Representative Speeches

Following this, New Life Movement Promotion Association representative Jiang Hao spoke about the importance of hygiene for individuals and the nation. Health Bureau representative Shen Qifeng spoke about the significance of the hygiene movement. Security Committee representative Yu Da spoke about summer hygiene. All of these speeches were concise and to the point. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock.

Closing Conference Affairs

After yesterday's closing ceremony, the hygiene exhibition was extended until 6 PM. The broadcasting and speeches were handled by You Jihua, Yu Qiaqing, and Yuan Liangzhou. The remaining exhibition stores were gradually dismantled, and the exhibits will be packed starting today. In general, all conference affairs will be completed and cleared up within the week. In addition, all cleaning matters within this hygiene movement venue were voluntarily undertaken by the New Life Cleaning Service Company at 1100 Edward Road. Their serious work and thoughtful service are deeply appreciated, and they are recommended. If all sectors have cleaning needs, they can directly entrust them to handle them, and they will definitely be very satisfied.

Fengpu and Songpu Ships Run Aground in the Yangtze River at the Same Time 113

Songpu Runs Aground While Trying to Rescue Fengpu; Remains Aground After Three Days

The Fengpu, a freighter of the Sanbei Company in Shanghai, weighs 191 tons, is 263 feet and 2 inches long, 38 feet and 3 inches wide, and has a draft of 16 feet and 2 inches. The ship was loaded with salt in Haizhou, heading for the Yangtze River. On June 27th, the ship was fully loaded with salt in Haizhou and set sail for the Yangtze River. When the ship reached the Sanshan area above Nanjing, near Dashengguan (navigators say that if one navigates to the north, one can pass without incident), the Fengpu pilot guided the ship on the south side. Due to the shallow water, the Fengpu

Suddenly Ran Aground The depth in front of the bow was measured to be only 12 feet, and the depth at the stern was only 13 feet, while the depth on the left and right sides was 16 feet. It turned out that there was a shallow sandbar there. The Fengpu was heavily loaded and had a deeper draft, (causing the ship to sink deep into the sandbar and unable to move. The shipowner, Qin Naxun, sent an urgent telegram to Shanghai to report and request rescue from upstream and downstream ships. The company's Songpu (1975 tons, 277 feet and 3 inches long, 18 feet draft) was also carrying salt from Haizhou and following behind. After the Fengpu ran aground, the Songpu received a distress signal and

Flew to Tow The plan was to tow the Fengpu out of the shallows. However, the shallow sandbar under Sanshan was quite large. The Songpu arrived behind the Fengpu, wanting to sail closer to tow it. However, the Songpu's draft was even deeper than the Fengpu's, and it was also fully loaded with salt, so it could not get close to the Fengpu and also ran aground. The two ships are now lined up one after the other, stranded in the middle of the river. The Songpu also has no way to escape. The Shanghai company, after receiving the report, has sent a telegram to negotiate rescue procedures. If they cannot escape on their own, they will have to hire barges to unload the cargo. Yesterday afternoon, the company received another telegram from the Fengpu, saying that the grounding was slightly looser and that they had consulted with the China Merchants Bureau.

Shanghai Post Offices to Issue Gift Certificates Today 114

Divided into Red and Plain Types with Four Denominations Can Be Redeemed for Cash at Local Post Offices Appointed Post Offices in Eighteen Provinces and Cities

The Shanghai Postal Administration and its affiliated branches have scheduled to start issuing Savings and Remittance Bureau gift certificates simultaneously from 9 AM today. These gift certificates are divided into red and plain types, with denominations of one yuan, two yuan, four yuan, and ten yuan. The Datong News Agency reporter has recorded the details from the bureau as follows: Simple Regulations for Issuing Gift Certificates The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau's simple regulations for issuing gift certificates consist of five articles, recorded as follows: The purpose of issuing postal savings and remittance bureau gift certificates (hereinafter referred to as gift certificates) is to be used as gifts for relatives and friends at weddings, funerals, and other celebrations, to avoid the exchange of cash. After receiving these gift certificates, relatives and friends can deposit them into savings accounts or exchange them for cash at the original issuing bureau and its designated post offices in the same area. They can also be used to purchase stamps, pay electricity bills, and other postal and telecommunications transactions at designated postal and telecommunications agencies. Gift certificates are divided into four denominations: one yuan, two yuan, four yuan, and ten yuan. Their values are printed on the face of the certificate. When used or exchanged, their value is the same as national currency. Gift certificates are divided into red and plain types, and each type is equipped with a corresponding colored envelope, which is given free of charge when purchasing gift certificates. The issuance of gift certificates is anonymous. Postal and telecommunications agencies recognize the holder of the certificate as the owner of the gift certificate, so gift certificates cannot be reported lost. The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau is the issuer of the gift certificates, and the use and exchange of gift certificates are guaranteed by the post office. Director of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, Shen Shuyu, July 1, 1936. Appointed Post Offices The local post offices that will handle these gift certificates have also been appointed, covering eighteen provinces and cities, and are extremely widespread. The locations and bureau names are recorded as follows: Jiangsu Nanjing Administration Bureau, Nanjing Savings and Remittance Branch Bureau, Wuxian, Zhenjiang, Tongshan, Wuxi, Anhui, Huairang Administration Bureau, Wuhu, Bengbu, Shanghai Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, Shanghai Administration Bureau, Beiping, Beiping Administration Bureau, Hebei, Tianjin Administration Bureau, Shanxi, Yangqu Administration Bureau, Henan, Kaifeng Administration Bureau, Zhengxian, Shaanxi, Xijing Administration Bureau, Shandong, Jinan Administration Bureau, Hubei, Hankou Administration Bureau, Hankou Savings and Remittance Branch Bureau, Wuchang, Yichang, Shashi, Hunan, Changsha Administration Bureau, Jiangxi, Nanchang Administration Bureau, Jiujiang, Zhejiang, Hangzhou Administration Bureau, Yin County, Shaoxing, Fujian, Minhou Administration Bureau, Xiamen, Guangdong Guangzhou Administration Bureau, Guizhou, Guiyang Administration Bureau. Branches of the above-mentioned bureaus that handle savings and remittance business also handle postal savings and remittance bureau gift certificates. Notice of Issuance Today Shanghai Postal Administration Director Zhapailin issued Notice No. 51 on savings and remittance affairs stating that starting today, the Administration Bureau's Business General Affairs Office and its affiliated branches in the city will simultaneously issue gift certificates in four denominations: one yuan, two yuan, four yuan, and ten yuan, further divided into red and plain types, so that purchasers can use them as gifts for celebratory occasions or condolences to friends and relatives. Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau gift certificates can be exchanged for cash or deposited into savings accounts at the original issuing bureau and the post offices in the same postal district that handle this business (the names of the bureaus can be inquired at the original issuing bureau). They can also be used at the above-mentioned post offices and telegram bureaus in the same location as postal and telecommunications transactions. To avoid any lack of awareness, this special notice is issued.

The Jiangyu Ship Will Attempt Rescue During High Tide; Whether It Will Succeed Is Unknown According to crew members from various Yangtze River ships that arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon, the waters slightly north of that area are extremely deep, and Yangtze River ships can usually pass without hindrance. However, now that the Fengpu and Songpu are both aground, right in the middle of the river, and have been stranded for three days and nights without escaping, it feels particularly frustrating.

South Station: Crushed Train Conductor's Legs and Feet 115

Wang Guozhen Injured While Working on Tracks; Life Hangs in the Balance

At 11:20 PM the night before, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway's No. 802 freight train from Hangzhou arrived at the West Branch of the Shanghai South Station and stopped on the fourth track. The train conductor, Wang Guozhen, a 35-year-old from Zhenjiang, along with freight staff and railway police, were inspecting the freight cars when, unexpectedly, a locomotive emerged from the South Station engine house and entered the fourth track from the third, preparing to connect and tow the freight train. Conductor Wang was working on the tracks, directly in its path, and unable to avoid it. He was struck by the locomotive, crushing his left leg and four toes on his right foot. He immediately collapsed to the ground in pain, bleeding profusely. The night shift station master immediately dispatched police officers to provide assistance and sent him to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. His injuries are severe, and his life hangs in the balance.

Ready-Made Telegrams and Attached Gift Certificate Procedures to be Implemented Simultaneously Today 116

One Eliminates the Sender's Need for Composition, One Meets Social Needs

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau announced that since the Ministry of Communications initiated social telegrams, sending them has become exceptionally popular. Considering social customs, the Ministry decided that in addition to telegrams, there is often a need to include monetary gifts. However, due to time constraints, composing telegrams can be inconvenient. Therefore, they specially created the social telegram with attached gift certificate procedure and pre-selected ready-made social telegram texts to facilitate their use. The above measures will be implemented starting today. Ready-made social telegrams can be sent from all branches of the city's telegraph bureau. However, social telegrams with attached gift certificates must be sent from the main telegraph bureau at the corner of Fuzhou Road and Sichuan Road or the branch office at 565 Minguo Road. The following are excerpts of important regulations for reference.

Attached Gift Certificate Regulations: The sender of a social telegram may request that a gift certificate issued by the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau be attached and delivered to the recipient by the receiving telegraph office. Both the sender's and recipient's locations are limited to places where the local post office issues such gift certificates.

Location Restrictions: "Jiangsu Province": Nanjing, Shanghai, Zhenjiang, Wuxian, Tongshan, Wuxi. "Zhejiang Province": Hangzhou, Yin County (Ningbo), Shaoxing. "Anhui": Huaining (Anqing), Wuhu, Bengbu. "Jiangxi Province": Nanchang, Jiujiang. "Hubei Province": Hankou, Wuchang, Yichang, Shashi. "Hunan Province": Changsha. "Fujian Province": Fuzhou, Xiamen. "Sichuan Province": Chengdu, Ba County (Chongqing). "Hebei Province": Beiping, Tianjin. "Shandong Province": Jinan, Qingdao, Yantai. "Henan Province": Kaifeng, Zheng County. "Shanxi Province": Yangqu (Taiyuan). "Shaanxi Province": Chang'an (Xi'an). "Guizhou Province": Guiyang.

Amount and Fees: Gift certificates are available in scarlet and plain colors, with amounts ranging from one to twenty national currency dollars. A handling fee of ten cents (national currency) is charged for each attached certificate. Using ready-made telegrams incurs a telegram fee of forty cents. Self-composed telegrams are charged at the regular social telegram rate (i.e., two cents per Chinese character, four cents per English word). The certificate can be used for deposits or cash withdrawals at the issuing post office and designated post offices, and can also be used to pay various postal and telecommunication transaction fees at postal and telecommunications agencies.

Construction of Venue

Yesterday, Xu Letian, the secretary of the association's preparatory office, told a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency that major domestic goods factories in the city, in view of rampant smuggling and the severe impact on the sales of domestic goods, and that such smuggled goods are often disguised and counterfeit domestic goods, making it easy for buyers to be deceived, want to provide citizens with a deep understanding of genuine domestic products and arouse their love for them, in order to curb the dumping of smuggled goods. Booth locations will be selected by lottery on the morning of the 5th, and factories will begin setting up. The opening ceremony will be held at 2 PM on the 6th, and famous people will be invited to broadcast speeches on various radio stations on that day.

Opium Smokers: License Renewal Period Closed Yesterday 118

Those Who Did Not Renew in Time May Still Voluntarily Renew

Regarding the city's opium smokers,

The deadline for the second phase of renewing opium smoking licenses expired on June 30th. A total of more than 18,000 opium smokers renewed their licenses. According to the first registration, the total number of opium smokers was 30,833, which means that one-third did not renew their licenses. Apart from those who voluntarily quit smoking and applied to cancel their licenses, there are those who did not renew their licenses due to various special reasons. Since the city is a major port for commerce, many travelers come and go, and some opium smokers are traveling abroad and unable to renew their licenses within the time limit. In order to be considerate of opium smokers, the bureau will still allow those who voluntarily come to renew their licenses afterwards to show leniency. If the bureau discovers anyone smoking privately without a license, they will be severely punished.

Rape of a Young Girl Case: Judge Discovers Truth Through Honest Inquiry 119

Declares Innocent Verdict in Court

Ruan Zhu's eight-year-old daughter, Ruan Amao, who lived in Yuehua Lane, Tilanqiao, Hongkou, was allegedly raped by her brother, Ruan Zhixiong (18 years old), at the beginning of last month. The case was transferred by the Hongkou Police Department to the First Special Court. After repeated trials, because it involved public morals, public attendance was prohibited. The case was originally scheduled to be pronounced this Monday (June 29th). However, the presiding judge, Xiao Xieifen, reviewed the entire case's testimony and noted that the Municipal Council Hospital found that the young girl's hymen had been ruptured and showed signs of venereal disease. Therefore, she reopened the debate and found that Ruan Zhu had twice accused Ruan Zhixiong of disobedience in the District Court, suggesting a negative feeling. After separate questioning, the testimonies of Ruan Amao and Ruan Zhu were inconsistent. She immediately declared the debate closed and pronounced Ruan Zhixiong not guilty in court.

Same Surname, Different Origin:

Xie-Qiu Estate Lawsuit

Qiu Rengao Issues a 50,000 Yuan Note; Pursuing Jewelry; Official Order to Transfer Files for Consultation

Qiu Rengao, a German doctor, is 43 years old and originally from Shangyu, Zhejiang. His ancestors moved to Shanghai to avoid the Red Turban Rebellion and settled there. It is said that his ancestor's original surname was Xie, and some say Wang. Rengao's father became an adopted son of the Qiu family, inheriting the Qiu surname, while his cousin Qingyuan still used the Xie surname. Qingyuan's first wife had three sons: Xien, Huien, and Qiaoen. His second wife had Enmei, Enjuan, and Enxin, three daughters who are currently studying. Qingyuan favored his second wife during his lifetime, so he put all his property under her control, and his children were not allowed to interfere. Rengao and the woman,

Belonging to Uncle and Sister-in-Law,

Completely disregarded suspicion and were unusually intimate. After Qingyuan's death, they became even more blatant and openly cohabited at 51 Bai'er Road in the French Concession, squandering Qingyuan's estate at will. Xien and his siblings knew but dared not speak out. In the summer of the year before last, seeing their mother seriously ill, fearing that once she passed away, they would not be able to investigate how much their father's estate was, they went to Dahua Hospital with their siblings to ask their stepmother. Rengao was also present. The woman, knowing she was dying,

Told her Children with Tears,

"All of your father's life savings are with your fourth uncle (referring to Rengao)." Rengao suddenly became displeased upon hearing the woman's words. Before the woman finished speaking, he interrupted with other words and immediately ordered Xien to go home with him, giving him a 50,000 yuan note. Xien knew that his father's estate was worth 100,000, so he was unwilling to accept the note for only half the amount. Rengao explained that the remaining money had been lost due to speculative business with the woman. Several days later, the woman died. Xien then took the 50,000 yuan note and demanded the money from Rengao, but Rengao repeatedly delayed. Last summer, he suddenly claimed that the note was written under duress by Xien using a gun and refused to acknowledge it. Xien felt that his uncle was trying to

Devour the Entire

Estate, and was unwilling to accept it. He joined his two brothers and three sisters to file a lawsuit against Qiu Rengao in the First Special District Court, demanding the return of the 50,000 yuan estate. A hearing was held once, but because Qiu insisted that the note was obtained by the plaintiff using violent coercion, causing criminal issues, the case was temporarily suspended. Afterwards, the uncle and nephew switched to the Shanghai District Court to fight another criminal lawsuit. Over a year has passed, the criminal case has been concluded after two trials by the Jiangsu Higher Court. Therefore,

The Old Matter is Raised Again,

Returning to the First Special Court to involve the lawsuit over the 50,000 yuan estate again. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Mo Runhua opened a court hearing. The defendant, Qiu Rengao, did not appear, and a lawyer appeared on his behalf. The plaintiffs, Xien, Huien, and Qiaoen brothers, and Enjuan and Enxin sisters, all presented themselves. Only Enmei was sick at home and could not attend. Xie Xien spoke on behalf of his siblings, briefly recounting the old situation, stating that his late father's property was entrusted to the defendant and his stepmother for management, totaling 80,000 in cash and land worth 20,000. The defendant and his stepmother had cohabited on Bai'er Road. After the stepmother died, her jewelry was also taken away. Therefore, in addition to suing for the return of the 50,000 yuan estate, all jewelry should also be returned. This case was previously mediated by Qian Zhongxiao and Chen Wencan,

Lawyer Mediation,

Requesting that those two be summoned to court, and they would be able to testify, etc. The defendant's lawyer immediately stated that the plaintiff's stepmother had previously divided more than 10,000 in cash among her three daughters, and the money was stored in the Xinkang Pawnshop on Broadway, which was opened by her maternal family. He also presented a note of 1,000 yuan that the plaintiff borrowed from his sister, stating that this was sufficient to show that the three daughters had already received cash. However, the plaintiff claimed that the Xinkang Pawnshop was not opened by his maternal family and that no money was stored there, and requested that the criminal case files be retrieved from the Shanghai District Court for verification. Judge Mo then ordered a change of date to July 16th in the morning for another hearing.

Man and Woman Committed Suicide by Poison in a Closed Room 120

Luo Fu Had a Husband, and the Envoy Had a Wife; Secret Love Could Not Last, Attempted Suicide by Poison and Were Saved

On June 25th, a middle-aged man and a young woman arrived at the Jincheng Hotel on Hankou Road and booked Room No. 2. The man claimed to be Zhao Yongbi, 36 years old, from Ningbo, and the woman was Cui Zhou, 19 years old. They were inseparable for days and extremely intimate. Observing their actions and laughter, they seemed like newlyweds. Even when they occasionally went out, they always went together. Unexpectedly, at around 1:30 AM yesterday morning, the tea server suddenly heard moaning and sobbing coming from the room, arousing great suspicion. He tried knocking on the door but received no response, so he managed to open the door and enter. He found both of them lying on the bed, with tears in their eyes, pale faces, and rapid breathing. However, they were still conscious. When asked why, they vaguely refused to answer. However, he glimpsed an empty container of poison, and he realized they had taken poison. He quickly reported to the police, who sent them to the hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the poisoning was mild, and they were saved. After questioning, they claimed that Zhao Yongbi was a fishmonger and already had a wife at home, while Cui Zhou was also already married. The two of them were united by secret love, and their passion reached a breaking point. Because it was difficult for their relationship to last, they attempted suicide by poison together.

City Suffering from Mosquitoes This Summer 121

Affecting Citizens' Health; Risk of Malignant Malaria

Shanghai, a large metropolis with towering buildings, rarely has mosquitoes in the summer. However, this year is different. Since the beginning of summer, mosquitoes have been rampant in areas such as South Shanghai, Zhabei, West Shanghai, and the British and French Concessions. They cannot be eliminated by swatting or chasing away. Their buzzing sound continues all night, not only disturbing people's sleep but also significantly affecting citizens' health. According to medical experts, malignant malaria will likely become widespread this year. Citizens should take precautions.

Fifteen People Fell into the Water, Two Survived

At around 5 PM the day before yesterday, a Chongming sailboat carrying fifteen passengers capsized off the coast of Wusong, in the Lao Yaokou river area. No ships were able to rescue them at the time, so they all drowned. It is reported that only the boat crew members, brothers Zhi Lilang and Zhi Genlang, swam to a nearby beach and escaped danger.

Male and Female Travelers Suddenly Abandon a Child at the Longsheng Hotel 123

Official Order Sent to Renji Orphanage for Care

At 1 PM on the 28th of this month, a man and a woman arrived at the Longsheng Hotel at No. 6, Lane 446, Fuzhou Road and booked Room No. 26. The man spoke with a Ningbo accent, was about 30 years old, and claimed to be Wang Zhichang. The woman's name was unknown. The two of them were dressed neatly. At the time, the woman was holding a child in her arms. They stayed for one night. At 3 PM the day before yesterday, the man and woman suddenly went out at the same time, not taking the child with them. When the tea server asked why they weren't taking the child with them, they replied that they would be back soon, so there was no need to take it out. By 7 PM that evening, the man and woman had not returned, and the child was crying non-stop. The hotel reported this to the Lao Zha Police Department, and Officer He Lianzeng was ordered to investigate. He saw a red cloth on the child's leg with the words "Wang Meimei, born at 7:15 AM on June 20th." It was clear that this child was an illegitimate child and that they would never return to claim it. Therefore, he took the child to the police station and fed it milk. Yesterday morning, he applied to the First Special District Court for disposal. After Judge Shen inquired about the situation, he ordered the child to be sent to the Renji Orphanage for care.

Some Claim to Have Closed; Some Sold to Japanese

Recently, the Xin Dalu Dance School at 548 Fuzhou Road, the Peach Blossom River Dance School in Taichang Building at 430 Zhejiang Road, and the Tao Tao Dance School at 852 Beijing Road were found selling dance tickets by Deputy Detective Zhang Mingde of the Lao Zha Police Department. The police prosecuted the heads of these three dance schools, Wu Ziliang, Tan Zhixiong, and Pan Guangliang. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen of the First Special Court's Arrest Police Court summoned them. Wu Ziliang of Xin Dalu did not appear and was ordered to be summoned again at a later date. Pan Guangliang of Tao Tao claimed that it had closed since June 26th, and the court ordered a change of date and ordered the police to investigate whether this was true before verifying it. Tan Zhixiong of Peach Blossom River claimed that the school had been sold to a Japanese, Endo Takato, for 2,500 yuan on the 8th of this month and presented a sale agreement as proof. Judge Shen ordered the police to investigate and change the date of this case for further verification.

Liu Haisu's Second European Tour: Exhibition Opens Today 125

More than 200 New Oil and Traditional Paintings; Liu's Work "Eagle Sea"

Contemporary painting master Liu Haisu (engaging in the New Art Movement for 28 years, Chinese painting history reached a major turning point with Mr. Liu. In 1929, he first toured Europe and exhibited calligraphy and paintings in Paris, and the French government purchased his paintings for the museum. The great writer Louis Laloy wrote an article calling him "The Master of the Chinese Renaissance." In 1933, Mr. Liu went to Europe for the second time to exhibit paintings, traveling through more than ten countries including Germany, the Netherlands, Switzerland, France, Italy, the United Kingdom, and Czechoslovakia, taking three years. He was welcomed enthusiastically everywhere he went, and the public opinion was excellent. German scholars Professor Quimai and Professor Frank, and the British critic Roland Spence, highly praised him, truly opening a new era never seen before internationally. The Berlin Daily and the London Times repeatedly published special articles on Mr. Liu's art, saying that if China had such culture and such creation, it would be irrational for us to attempt invasion. The German and French governments specially opened rooms in the Berlin and Paris National Museums to display Mr. Liu's works. His brilliance still shines before the Europeans. In addition to exhibiting paintings, Mr. Liu also worked hard at creation. He returned to China last autumn and went to Mount Huang and other scenic spots to continue producing works. He has collected 300 new works (the content is divided into two parts: traditional Chinese paintings and oil paintings, many of which were created in Berlin, London, Paris, Switzerland, and after returning to China) to hold a second European tour exhibition in Shanghai. It opens today at the New Building on the fourth floor of the Great New Company on Nanjing Road, and will be exhibited for fifteen days. The opening ceremony will be hosted by President Cai of the Academia Sinica at 4 PM, and Mayor Wu will be invited to unveil it. Tea parties have also been invited for famous people and people from all walks of life at home and abroad. Minister of Education Wang Shijie wrote a preface, saying, "Mr. Haisu inherited the family tradition and made years of efforts. He has already integrated ancient and modern famous paintings and is valued by the world. He is still not modest and believes that he has not exhausted the world's spectacle and is not enough to show his talent. Therefore, he has traveled across the oceans again and again, and has visited famous monuments in countries such as England, France, Italy, Germany, Belgium, and Switzerland, and has extensively read Greek and Roman literature, combining realism and charm in one furnace to complete his unique style. While traveling and writing, he depicts the strange landscapes, magnificent buildings, and complex social conditions of Europe in his paintings. His masterpieces have been exhibited in European countries and major cities in our country, and have been greatly praised by celebrities at home and abroad. The Berlin and Paris Museums of Art have also opened special rooms to display his works, which is a special event in the international art world. Now he is opening an exhibition of his second European tour works in Shanghai, and those who view it can see the arduousness of his struggle and the ability to create, and his works must be respected and inspired. It is estimated that the opening of this meeting will not only increase the author's personal honor, but also have a great impact on the development of Chinese painting art. Therefore, I write a few words to introduce it to the world."

Liu's Work "Eagle Sea"

Textile Expert Li Zhuangshou Returns from Study in Japan 126

Mr. Li Zhuangshou, technical expert of the National Economic Council's Cotton Industry Control Committee and full-time researcher at the National Central Research Institute's Cotton Textile Dyeing Experimental Hall, was dispatched in January of last year to lead technicians Li Xuerui, Deng Hengxing, Cai Gufu, Liu Yujun, and others to Japan for study. They have all returned to China one after another in the past year and a half. Mr. Li graduated from the Dyeing and Weaving Department of Kiryu Advanced Industrial School in Japan. He used to be an engineer at Hengfeng Textile New Bureau. He currently holds this position. Because he felt the decline of the domestic textile industry, he unloaded his heavy responsibility and concentrated on research. He spent the longest time studying with Toyota Automatic Loom Works, Central Textile Co., Ltd., Toyota Textile Co., Ltd., and Enshu Automatic Loom Manufacturing Co., Ltd. He had a detailed investigation of the affairs of new-style factories. He also paid special attention to the factory. He then went to visit the newest factories in various parts of the country. With the advanced nature of the textile industry in that country and Mr. Li's spirit of hard work, he has now returned fully loaded, and will definitely contribute to the textile industry in our country.

Renji Hospital May Report 136

The Renji Hospital on Shandong Road, Maijiaquan, reports for May of this year: 14,076 outpatient visits, 340 new admissions, and a total of 6,178 inpatients. The daily average number of meals provided was 450. There were 56 male and 40 female suicide cases. 311 emergency treatments were performed, including 44 cases of injuries sustained in factories. The most prevalent disease this month was intermittent fever. Zhao Junhao's New Book "Ten Records of a Southern Journey" Published 138

Mr. Zhao Junhao, a reporter for this newspaper, was invited by the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section of the Guangdong-Han Railway Engineering Bureau in March of this year to inspect the construction situation and visit the scenic spots and historical sites along the route. His itinerary started from Shanghai, went up the Yangtze River to Hankou, and then south along the Guangdong-Han Railway to Guangzhou. Along the way, he passed through various places, such as Changsha, Zhuzhou, Lukou, Hengshan, Nanling, Hengyang, Chenzhou, Yizhang, Pingshi, Lechang, and Guangzhou. From Guangzhou, he visited Macau, Zhongshan, Hong Kong, and other places. After returning to Shanghai, he wrote "Ten Records of a Southern Journey," which includes: "The Joy of Traveling on the River," "One Day in Changsha," "The Lukou Bridge," "Climbing Nanling," "Hengyang News," "Chenshan Chenshui," "Mountains, Waters, Bridges, and Caves," "Guangzhou Scenic Spots," "Macau and Zhongshan," and "Hong Kong Tourism," totaling about 50,000 words. The book has now been published. Each record is accompanied by exquisite illustrations, totaling fifty images. The landscape painting by Han Che of the Guangdong-Han Railway is printed in three colors, making it particularly beautiful. The book's writing is beautiful, the descriptions are detailed, and the events recorded are very interesting. It is truly a masterpiece among travelogues. The retail price is 60 cents in legal tender per copy. It is sold at the Shanghai Shenbao Office, China Travel Service, Life Bookstore, Kaiming Bookstore, and Shanghai Magazine Company. For mail orders from other locations, full postage stamps can be used as payment, and no shipping fee is required. Those who love Zhao Junhao's works and are concerned about the situation along the Guangdong-Han Railway should be the first to read it.

The 100th inspection report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states that the committee, in accordance with the regulations, inspected the issuance and reserve vaults of the Shanghai Bank of China (including its branches) on June 28, 1936, with Dai Mingfeng, Director of the Monetary Department of the Ministry of Finance, Wang Yansong and Pei Yunqing, representatives of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Qu Jigang and Zhuang Dezhi, representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association, Liu Wuqiao and Zhang Wenbo, representatives of the Shanghai Money Trade Association, Xu Jiji and Li Shida, representatives of various banks and firms issuing coupons, and accountant Wang Zikang present. The inspection results are listed as follows: Total amount of coupons issued: 237,851,380 yuan, including 145,147,842 yuan issued by the Bank of China itself, 64,478,543 yuan used by branch banks, and 28,224,995 yuan used by various banks and firms. Total amount of coupon reserves: 237,851,380 yuan, including 155,229,566.19 yuan in cash reserves and 82,621,813.81 yuan in guarantee reserves. The cash reserves account for more than 60%, and the guarantee reserves account for less than 40%. The above amounts were verified to be accurate. This is hereby officially reported. June 28, 1936, Republic of China.

The Nanhua Industry of Shanghai 149

— Edited by China Credit

1. Development: The Nanhua industry of Shanghai dates back to the Daoguang era of the late Qing Dynasty. At that time, the areas inside and outside the city walls were extremely desolate and sparsely populated. The scope of the first businesses was small, only dealing in oil, wine, porridge, soy sauce, incense, candles, paper horses, etc., which were commonly known as grocery stores. However, the area east of the Dawang Temple on Guajie Street on the Bund was relatively lively because it was close to the Huangpu River, with convenient boat traffic. As more residents moved in, merchants established markets, and after 30 years of hard work, the area gradually became a bustling street. During the Xianfeng era, the area expanded to Laoma Road, and the areas from 60th Avenue to Dongjiadu also became market areas. Business grew year by year, and by the Tongzhi era, it had become the most prosperous street. It is said that large-scale Nanhua stores such as Tongfeng, Tongtai, Laotaisheng, Xintaisheng, Tongfa, Nansanmao, Beisanmao, Hongtai, and Xiantai were established, specializing in famous domestic products from various provinces, including southern and northern groceries, Fujian and Guangdong brown sugar, Guanshan peaches and dates, and Eastern and Western ocean products (i.e., Western seafood), providing everything needed by society. The first entrepreneurs were the Zhou family from Huzhou. Later, the number of businesses increased, and there were two groups: the Huzhou group and the local group. However, the Huzhou group accounted for most of the industry, so it was considered the top group in the industry.

2. Scope of the Nanhua Industry and Its Relationship with Beihuo: China is a vast country with abundant resources. Therefore, the scope of southern and northern goods is quite broad. Products from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Fujian, Sichuan, and Guangdong are called Nanhua (Southern goods). Products from Liaoning, Jilin, Hebei, Shandong, Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, Henan, etc., are called Beihuo (Northern goods). However, people generally refer to Nanhua stores and rarely refer to Beihuo stores. There is a reason for this. In the late Qing Dynasty, the main business of Nanhua stores was red and white sugar. The source of sugar was mainly from Fujian and Guangdong, and also from Taiwan. At that time, Taiwan had not been occupied by Japan and was part of southern China. Therefore, it was called Fujian, Guangdong, and Taiwan sugar. As a result, it became a common practice to simply call them Nanhua stores.

3. Names and Sources of Nanhua Products: Guangdong coarse-grained white sugar, medium-grained white sugar, cotton white sugar, sliced green sugar; Shantou green sugar, red sugar, white sugar, coarse-grained white sugar, medium-grained white sugar, Ru flour; Guangxi sliced green sugar, original Tong, Xinhui peel; Fujian rock sugar, red sand, green sugar, white sugar, green Tong, fragrant mushrooms, longans, lychees, Yuan jade, cinnamon, persimmon cakes, Linba Tingjian; Xiaofeng Qi Xun, Yi Jian; Hangzhou Tianmu bamboo shoots; Anhui honey dates, Tunxi fragrant mushrooms; Lanxi fragrant mushrooms; Changshan white lotus; Jinhua southern ham, southern dates; Suzhou southern gordon euryale seeds; Ningbo light Zhuyu, razor clams, fish lips, yellow belly slices, Fan skirt, Sanmao belly, leather knife cotton skirt, Jiwei, pirates, seaweed, Ru flour, vermilion face, southern pepper; Sichuan pickled mustard tuber, silver ear fungus; Yunnan big-headed vegetable, Sichuan bamboo shoots.

4. Names and Sources of Beihuo Products: The scope of Beihuo is very broad. All products from Guandong, Sichuan-Han, Liaoyang, Tianjin, etc., are called Beihuo. Tianjin chestnuts, red dates, walnuts, melon seeds, white melon seeds, sunflower seeds, almonds, dried shrimp; Henan daylily, melon seeds, big-headed vegetables, Xian rice; Shandong melon seeds, gum, black dates, persimmon cakes, Geng cakes, raw kernels, peanuts, Fufu flour, vermicelli, spiced vegetables, Chinese toon vegetables, date winter vegetables, chestnuts, yellow lip gum; Guandong pine nuts, yellow hemp, red flag ginseng, deer cap, ugly cap, frog oil, rice kernels; Zhangjiakou mushrooms, melon seeds; Hunan Xianglian, melon seeds; Yantai dried scallops, shrimp tails, shrimp roe, Nanzi, raw kernels, peanuts; Xuzhou daylily, melon seeds, raw kernels, peanuts; Xishan melon seeds; Bozhou red dates, daylily; Luhe pumpkin seeds; Jining melon seeds, black dates; Yangzhou sesame seeds.

5. Eastern Goods Included in Nanhua: Shark fin, bird's nest, bird skin, bird sheep, shrimp tails, Yuan Dong tails, flat Dong tails, agar, seaweed (three types: large square, medium square, and small square), dried scallops, Eastern dried mussels, Ten-fan ginseng, squid, kelp, shredded kelp, bright abalone, sea bandits, dried razor clams, monosodium glutamate, Eastern Tong, green snails, Che sugar (divided into four-temperature half, four-temperature, three-temperature half, three-temperature, two-temperature half, etc.).

6. Western Goods Included in Nanhua: White swallow's nest, hairy swallow's nest, Ji Yu Ji wings, bald sea cucumber, jade sea cucumber, red sea cucumber, squid, Jinshan tail, Mumbai tail, pile wings, cornstarch, Western dried mussels, saccharin, foreign soda, sandalwood, Jiangxiang, train white sugar (divided into five-temperature, four-temperature half, four-temperature, three-temperature half, three-temperature, two-temperature half six types), green sugar, red sugar, rock sugar, black and white Dachuan. (To be continued)

Education News

Ministry of Education Orders: Elementary Schools Must Not Use Outdated Textbooks 164

And Must Not Use Unapproved Books or Have Children Copy Fragmented Materials

(Nanjing, 30th) – The Ministry of Education has ordered all provincial and municipal education bureaus that the new elementary school teaching subjects, weekly teaching schedule, and common knowledge curriculum standards have been announced by the Ministry. The elementary school textbooks for the three subjects of society, nature, and hygiene, which were edited by various publishers according to the old standards, are no longer valid. Hereafter, elementary schools must not continue to use them. Furthermore, civic training is a form of moral education that is implemented in practice, and there is absolutely no need to use textbooks. All civic training textbooks published by various publishers must not be used by elementary schools. It is hereby ordered that this be known and passed on to all subordinate elementary schools for compliance.

The Ministry of Education also ordered all provincial and municipal education bureaus that elementary school textbooks and books should use the versions approved by the Ministry, as has been clearly stipulated. Recently, it has been found that some elementary schools in various regions have failed to fully comply, or have arbitrarily used unapproved versions or self-compiled textbooks without approval, or have not used textbooks at all, but instead have had children copy fragmented materials. The errors in the materials are too numerous to count, which is a violation of regulations and harms children's learning. Hereafter, elementary schools should each choose textbooks and books that have been approved by the Ministry, except for those specifically permitted by the Ministry. In addition to self-compiled supplementary materials, they must not use unapproved self-compiled textbooks, and must not constantly have children copy fragmented materials. School inspectors and supervisors should strictly review and inspect, and if they encounter situations where unapproved versions and unapproved self-compiled textbooks are being used, they should correct them. Those who do not comply may be requested by the competent educational administrative organ to discipline their principals or directors. It is hereby ordered that this be known and passed on to all subordinates for compliance.

Ministry of Education Explains Compendium of Educational Laws and Regulations 168

The Ministry of Education recently explained educational laws and regulations, which are compiled below:

Regarding the Sichuan Provincial Government's inquiry about the method of calculating physical education and scout scores in junior high schools, the province was informed that, based on the request from the Baisha Town District Girls' Junior High School in Jiangjin County, the method of calculating scout and physical education scores should be specified. After investigation, it was found that the teaching time for physical education and scouts in junior high schools is two hours each. Scouts have an additional hour of extracurricular training. According to these regulations, both physical education and scouts must pass, and then the average is calculated as the physical education and scout score. Correspondingly, this is communicated in response.

In response to the request from the Huai River Conservancy Committee to recognize the qualifications of graduates of the training class for engineering personnel, stating that the level of the training class for engineering personnel is only equivalent to a short-term vocational training class, and its graduates cannot be recognized as having the qualifications of a specialized school graduate. The original letter stated, "Approved letter, reporting to request retroactive recognition of the qualifications of the training class graduates," and attached relevant documents for review. After investigation, it was found that the training class for engineering personnel was specifically established to train engineering personnel for the Huai River Conservancy, and the duration of study is this year. The level is only equivalent to a short-term vocational training class, and its graduates cannot be recognized as having the qualifications of a specialized school graduate. Except for the attached documents, which will be filed for future reference, this is communicated in response for your information.

Scout Cadre Training Class Graduates 172

President Chiang Presents Certificates and Awards, Delivering an Instruction Speech

The Scout Cadre Training Class of the General Association of China Scouts held a graduation ceremony for the students on the 29th. President Chiang Zhongzheng, Chen Lifu, Lu Chao, Wang Shijie, and the students attended. After the ceremony, Chiang presented certificates and awards and gave an instruction speech, stating that soldiers must be upright in their words and deeds, and live a hard and frugal life. This is the fundamental principle of being a person. As those responsible for training scouts, they should especially achieve this, so as to be a model for others and train children and young people. He also read out the party members' code of conduct and the articles for soldiers to study, earnestly urging and encouraging them. Director Zhang Zhizhong was unable to attend due to illness, but specially wrote an instruction to encourage them.

Shanghai Reading Room of the Chinese International Library Opens 175

The Chinese International Library was established by Wu Zhihui and Li Shi, with the aim of promoting cultural exchange between China and the West. The library has branches in Shanghai and Geneva. The Geneva branch has already opened, while the Shanghai branch is still actively preparing. To meet the needs of the reading community, the magazine section, which has been sorted, will be opened first on July 1st. The hours are from 9 AM to 9 PM, non-stop throughout the day, and it is said that there will be no holidays throughout the year. Once the book section has been sorted, it will also be opened to the public. The library currently has about 500 Chinese and Japanese magazines and about 100 Western magazines, which is a rich collection. All circles are welcome to visit and read. The magazine room is housed in a building built by the martyr Huang Keqiang, with a quiet environment and elegant decoration. The address is 1836 Avenue Joffre, near Route Ferguson. University Students Prepare to Go Abroad 176

Most Going to the US This Year, Followed by England and Germany

With the end of the 24th year, it has been learned that the number of graduates from universities across the country going abroad at their own expense or on government scholarships this summer is even greater than in previous years. The Global Student Association and the Association of British Students in this city are busy with the work of handling procedures for going abroad.

Large Number of Students Preparing to Go Abroad

With the end of the academic year, graduates from public and private colleges and universities in China are preparing to go abroad for further study. Reporters have inquired at relevant agencies and learned that the number of students going to the United States this year, whether at their own expense or on government scholarships, will be over 200. The number of students going to Germany and England is also higher than in previous years. Fewer students are going to France and Belgium, and only one or two are going to Italy and Denmark. As for the subjects studied, engineering is the most popular, followed by political science and economics, while those studying liberal arts are a minority.

Applying for Study Abroad Certificates

Many students are not clear about the procedures for applying for study abroad certificates from the Ministry of Education. The Global Student Association has issued the following statement: When applying for study abroad certificates from the Ministry of Education, students in Japan must have a diploma; only graduates of colleges and universities are eligible. Two photos, a certificate stamp fee of three yuan, a letter of guarantee, and a bank or agency deposit certificate are required. The documents required in Europe and the United States are the same as in Japan, but there is no need to submit a deposit certificate. The procedures for applying for a passport are relatively simple. If there is anything unclear, you can inquire with the association for all information.

Latest Departure Date for Europe is August

Students going to Europe this year must depart no later than early August, as the academic year in European universities always begins in mid-October or early November. Those studying in the United States must first obtain a certificate of admission from the school they wish to enter before proceeding with other procedures for going abroad. Students studying in the United States should pay attention to this.

Shen Bao National Products Special

Student National Products Movement During the Summer Vacation 182

Time flies like water. In an instant, the summer vacation of the 25th year of the Republic has begun again. As schools at all levels begin their summer vacations, I have boundless hopes for the many enthusiastic and promising young people. I earnestly and sincerely hope that all ambitious young students, in addition to working hard to improve their studies during the summer vacation, will also devote some energy and time to working for the National Products Movement, so that our National Products Movement, thanks to the efforts of you young students, will show particularly outstanding results during the summer season. How to do it? In my opinion, there are several items below.

Organize National Products Propaganda Groups: Promoting national products requires a strong emphasis on propaganda. During the summer vacation, young students can contact nearby classmates or ambitious young people from their hometown to organize a national products propaganda group. They can go out to promote national products once a day or every other day, so that their fellow villagers deeply understand the importance of promoting national products and recognize the dangers of using foreign goods. I believe that with the students' sincere attitude, fluent speech, and exemplary spirit, the results of this national products propaganda group will be considerable.

Inspect Household Items: Promoting national products must start from the family, and then it will have a significant effect. Many families can buy and use national products, but there are also many who are misled and mistakenly use foreign goods. During the summer vacation, young students can inspect the items in their homes. Which are national products? Which are not national products? A standard must be set, and the products of various national products factories, as well as their trademarks and addresses, should be promoted. In this way, most of the things used in the family in the future will surely be able to abandon foreign goods and buy national products.

Promote the Situation of Smuggling: The problem of smuggling is now really serious! How can we make the general public recognize the seriousness of smuggling? How can we make the general public determined not to buy smuggled goods? Not to use smuggled goods? This is a very important issue at present. Young students should use their summer vacation to conduct a general propaganda on the issue of smuggling, so that tens of thousands of people in various places can unanimously know the seriousness of smuggling and advise each other not to buy smuggled goods. This is a very urgent matter.

In short, the national crisis is so critical, and the national products industry is so precarious. You promising young students should spend your time during the summer vacation in a serious manner. How can it be enough to only work hard for the National Products Movement!

Contributing to the Promotion Group of National Products 183

— Yang An

The development of national products depends half on manufacturing and half on promotion. The responsibility of manufacturing rests with the factories, and the responsibility of promotion rests with everyone. The organization of national products promotion groups is especially powerful. The mission of a national products promotion group has four points:

Go to each school to promote student supplies, taking the opportunity to promote the main points of promoting and using national products.

Go to each household to promote household goods, spread throughout the residences of each alley and each neighborhood, and have sincere talks with housewives. Make them thoroughly understand the benefits of using national products, and get used to using national products, and establish a very good relationship with each other. From then on, if each family does not use goods, then so be it, but if they do use goods, they must wait for the promoters to come to their door.

Go to each village and each village, so that the general public knows that national products are exquisite and more beneficial than using foreign goods, and cultivate the spirit that rural people "do not use national products if they are not national products, and do not use national products if they are not national products."

Go to various institutions, groups, and factories and shops in industry and commerce, and persuade clerks, shop assistants, workers, and apprentices to use national products, so as to avoid the unemployment of workers and the collapse of industry and commerce.

The promotion of national products must have the phenomenon of mercury pouring on the ground, entering everywhere. Then the territory of national products will become wider day by day, and the livelihood of national products will become more and more. There are four conditions for promoters:

(1) Be able to endure hardship and suffering, especially be able to hold your breath.

(2) Be able to have in-depth skills, adapt to the situation, speak the language of the school when you arrive at the school, talk about the situation of the family when you go to the family, talk about supplements when you see the elderly, and look at toys when you see children. This is the skill that promoters should have. It is heard that a certain promoter is good at this method, and can do 30 yuan of business every day.

(3) Be able to investigate, where you are used to using a certain thing, where you are used to eating a certain product, cater to people's preferences, and suit people's tastes. This kind of skill is indispensable.

(4) Comply with social psychology, say a certain word when you arrive at a certain place, and when you sell a certain product, you should test the authenticity of the product. Especially, you must start from the psychology of the masses. In short, it is easy to deal with things, but difficult to deal with things, but I don't know that it is more difficult to deal with people. The saying that conforms to social psychology seems easy, but it is very difficult to implement.

Now Kangyuan Canned Food Factory has also adopted the method of withdrawing promoters, entrusting the China Vocational Education Society to handle it. It is beneficial to manufacturers without any harm, and it can also maintain thousands and hundreds of unemployed people, so that users can get safe and satisfactory products, and everyone who is unemployed has something to do. This is the fundamental problem of solving the unemployed, and it must not be regarded as a hopeless work. This promising future is in the golden rule of promoters. I hope that manufacturers will continue to believe in it to benefit the unemployed compatriots.

"Summer" and National Products 184

— Xuan Wan

The progression of time has not been slowly supported and slipped away because of our "economic national crisis." When we see the temperature of the thermometer rising day by day, and modern girls have already put on Qiao Qisha cheongsams, and parade on the streets with their bare toes, we know that the summer of the "National Products Year for Citizens" has come again.

However, here, I seem to be nervously thinking again, according to past facts and experiences, under the national's widespread worship of foreign goods psychology, the beginning of that summer is precisely giving foreign goods a good opportunity to dump their goods. Like imported and georgette yarns and silk fabrics! Soda! Beer! Dark fragrance! Electric fans! Straw hats! T-shirts! These many things are about to be very active in our country's market at this time, scouring a huge amount of our great money.
